om namaḥ śrī ugratārāyai

prakaṭavikaṭadaṃṣṭrā ghorarudrāṭṭahāsā naraśirakṛtamālā meghagambhīrarāvā ।
tribhuvanajanadhātrī khaḍgavinyastahastā karakaratikapālā pātu va ugratārā ।।

ghorarūpe mahārāve sarvaśatrukṣayaṅkari ।
bhaktebhyo varade devi trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

surāsurārcite devi siddhagandharvasevite ।
jāḍyapāpahare devi trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

sarvamaṇḍala sarvasattvahite anaghe ।
siddhānāṃ pūjite devi trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

ghorarūpasthite devi sarvaprāṇahare stute ।
ugratāre namo nityaṃ trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

jaṭājūṭasamāyukte lalajjihvordhvakāriṇi ।
drutabuddhiprade devi trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

somarūpe koṭṭarūpe candrarūpe namo astu te ।
śaktirūpe namastubhyaṃ trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

jaḍo ahaṃ śaktihīno ahaṃ na tavādhigame kṣamaḥ ।
mando mandamatiścāhaṃ trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

snāne dāne tathā jāpye balidāne tathā kratau ।
prasthāne ca na śakto ahaṃ trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

śaktihīnamanāthaṃ ca sarvapāpasamanvitam ।
tvāṃ vinā na gatiryasya trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

gaurī lakṣmīrmahāmāyā umā devī sarasvatī ।
sarvāstvameva he mātastrāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। 

gandhapuṣpādidravyaiśca vandhanādibhireva ca ।
devīṃ sampūjya yatnena labhate vāñchitaṃ phalam ।। 

aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ navamyāṃ yaḥ paṭhennaraḥ ।
paramāṃ siddhimāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

mokṣārthī labhate mokṣaṃ dhanārthī labhate dhanam ।
vidyārthī labhate vidyāṃ tarkavyākaraṇādikām ।। 

idaṃ stotraṃ paṭhitvā tu saṃgrāme praviśennaraḥ ।
tasya śatruḥ kṣayaṃ yāti sadā prajñā prajāyate ।। 

pīḍāyāmatha saṃdhāne vipadāyāṃ tathā bhaye ।
ya idaṃ paṭhate stotraṃ śubhaṃ tasya na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

śrīmahogratārāstutiḥ samāptā ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no maṅgalaṣoḍaśastutiḥ

om namaḥ samantabhadrāya

yena puṇyāṭavīsthenāneke śāsanavartinaḥ ।
divodāsādayo bhūpāḥ sa no rakṣatu mārajit ।। 

lokānāṃ grahabaddhānāṃ rakṣārthaṃ puṇyakānane ।
grahānadamayad yo vai sa no rakṣatu tadbhayāt ।। 

kāśyapādyān maharṣīṃstān ānandādyāṃśca brāhmaṇān ।
prāvrājayat sumuktyarthaṃ sa no rakṣatu muktidaḥ ।। 

sauvarṇadhānyadānena dīnaṃ vipramapālayat ।
durbhikṣabhayato nityaṃ sa no rakṣatu śākyarāṭ ।। 

yo maitrakanyako bhūtvā mātṛdrohiṇamatyagāt ।
cakraṃ dūrīkṛtaṃ yena sa no rakṣatu mātṛvān ।। 

supriyo badaradvīpayātrāptamaṇivṛṣṭibhiḥ ।
kāśīyān prākarodāḍhyān sa no rakṣatu kāñcanaiḥ ।। 

bhūtvā yaḥ sudhano nāma nidhānaṃ samadarśayat ।
dāridrayaduḥkhato nityaṃ sa no rakṣatu sarvavit ।। 

kuṣṭhādirogaharaṇe rājagṛhamupāviśat ।
tattadrogabhayānnityaṃ sa no rakṣatu dharmarāṭ ।। 

yaḥ kuśo bhūpatirbhūtvā aṣṭamīmāhātmyamuttamam ।
prakāśayannije dehe sa no rakṣatu dharmavit ।। 

saudāsaṃ satyavacasā kāśyāmasthāpayannṛpān ।
bandhanānmocayāmāsa sa no rakṣatu sarvavit ।। 

gopān rarakṣa yo devyāḥ prabhāvaṃ saṃprakāśayan ।
vahnidāhāribhayataḥ sa no rakṣatu bhītihā ।। 

yo andhībhūtāṃ mātaraṃ svāṃ cūḍāratnaṃ jale vyadhāt ।
divyanetrān janān kṛtvā sa no rakṣatu netradaḥ ।। 

virūpaṃ prākarot putraṃ chāyāsīnaṃ susundaram ।
sarvalakṣaṇasampannaṃ sa no rakṣatu sarvadaḥ ।। 

sakalānandanāmānaṃ rājye yaḥ prābhyaṣecayat ।
santatisthitikurvāṇaḥ sa no rakṣatu sthairyakṛt ।। 

viṣadaṃ bhrātaraṃ yaścākṣamad bhikṣun viṣāśinaḥ ।
rarakṣa dhāraṇīvijñaḥ sa no rakṣatu nirviṣaḥ ।। 

śrīsvayaṃbhudarśanāya naipālīyān prayāsitum ।
kapilān prasthito yo asau sa no rakṣatu santatam ।। 

bhadrakalpāvadānoddhṛtā śākyasiṃhasya maṅgalaṣoḍaśastutiḥ samāptā ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no maṅgalāṣṭakam

mañjuśrīrlokanātho jinavaramakuṭo jambhalo vajrasattva maitreyo vajrapāṇiḥ sukhakarakamalo rāhulo bhadrapālaḥ ।
buddho vairocanādyastribhuvananamitaḥ kṣīṇaniḥśeṣadoṣastuṣṭāḥ sarvārthasiddhiṃ dadatu samarasā maṅgalaṃ bodhisattvāḥ ।। 

hṛṣṭo hūṃkāravajraḥ paśupatidamako vajraghaṇṭā ca hṛṣṭ pīto hālāhalāsyo ripugaṇamathano ṭakkirājo mahātmā ।
akṣobhyo ratnaketuḥ pratidinamacalo gaṇḍahastiryamāristuṣṭāḥ sarvārthasiddhiṃ dadatu samarasā maṅgalaṃ bodhisattvāḥ ।। 

saṃghastrailokyabandhurguṇagaṇanilayo bodhicittaḥ sucittaḥ bodhiścānandasiddho vijitakalimalo heruko nīladaṇḍaḥ ।
buddhaḥ sāraṅgarājo vijitajinaguṇo sarvasattvānukampī tuṣṭāḥ sarvārthasiddhiṃ dadatu samarasā maṅgalaṃ bodhisattvāḥ ।। 

prajñā candrāvatārā tadanujabhṛkuṭī jñānasaṃbhārabhār mārīcī māramārā sakalabhayaharā pītavarṇā trivaktrā ।
māyūrī māmakī ca kṣapitaripugaṇā pāṇḍarā rocanādyāstuṣṭāḥ sarvārthasiddhiṃ dadatu samarasā maṅgalaṃ bodhisattvāḥ ।। 

gāndhārī jāṅgulī ca bhujagahṛtaphaṇā khaḍgapāśāṅkuśogrā vārāhī vajrahastā asiparaśudharā dharmadhātvīśvarī ca ।
keyūrī jñānasārā dhvajanihitakarā ṣaṭkarā śābarī ca tuṣṭāḥ sarvārthasiddhiṃ dadatu samarasā maṅgalaṃ bodhisattvāḥ ।। 

vaiṇyā mālyā sugītā prathitajinavare śābarī dhūpavajrā vaitālī gandhavajrā prahasitavadanā svargatirāryatārā ।
lakṣmīrbuddhasya bodhiḥ sakalabhayaharā śāradā dīpavajrā tuṣṭāḥ sarvārthasiddhiṃ dadatu samarasā maṅgalaṃ bodhisattvāḥ ।। 

vaiśālyāṃ dharmacakre prathitanijabale parvate gṛdhrakūṭe śrāvastyāṃ lumbinīke kṣitinihitakarā koṃkaṇe bodhivṛkṣā ।
śrīvatsāśvatthapatraṃ suravaranamitaṃ śrīphalaṃ śaṅkhacakraṃ tuṣṭāḥ sarvārthasiddhiṃ dadatu samarasā maṅgalaṃ bodhisattvāḥ ।। 

chatraṃ dūrvā ca padmaṃ dhvajamapi nihitaṃ lo canā matsyakūrma vārāhaḥ pūrṇakumbho munivaravacanaṃ vajraghaṇṭāninādaḥ ।
buddhānāṃ prātihāryaṃ suravaranamitaṃ hāsyalāsye vilāsāstuṣṭāḥ sarvārthasiddhiṃ dadatu samarasā maṅgalaṃ bodhisattvāḥ ।। 

maṅgalāṣṭakaṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no mañjuśrīstotram

śrīmañjunāthakamalāsanaratnamaulirvidyādhipo bhuvanamaṇḍalacakravartī ।
dhyānādhipocitavirājitasaumyarūpo vandāmahe suranarāsuravanditāryam ।। 

bālākṛtiḥ kuvalayojjvalalolahastaḥ keyūrahāramaṇikuṇḍalaghṛṣṭagaṇḍaḥ ।
khādaṃśca ṣoḍaśaradaṃ sukumārarūpaṃ vandāmahe suravarārcitamañjughoṣam ।। 

romāgrakūpavivare parivartamānaṃ viśvaprapañcakaraṇaṃ sugatātmajasya ।
traividyamantra tava nātha guṇārṇaveṇa sūkṣmāya buddhatanayāya namo astu tasmai ।। 

gambhīradharmanayamārgasukhapratiṣṭhaṃ jñānodadhiṃ nikhilasattvakṛtārthakāram ।
prajñānidhānaguṇasāgaramaprameyaṃ mañjuśriyaṃ jinasutaṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

viditasakalatattvaḥ kṣiptasantāpasattvastribhuvana upakārī sarvaduḥkhāpahārī ।
madanamathanavīraścārurūpaḥ sucīrastribhuvanajanatoṣaḥ pātu māṃ mañjughoṣaḥ ।। 

bālendurucirābhāsaṃ varābharaṇabhūṣitam ।
prajñābjāmalapatrākṣaṃ vande mañjuśriyaṃ sadā ।। 

pātraṃ vāmakare yasya bhramannañjalisaṃnibham ।
nāmnā te sarvato lakṣmīrmañjughoṣaṃ namāmyaham ।। 

khaḍgapustakahastāya candramaṇḍalavartine ।
ajñānadhvāntasūryāya mañjughoṣāya te namaḥ ।। 

jñānottaraprabhāketuṃ praṇidhānamatiṃ tathā ।
śāntendriyaṃ mañjughoṣaṃ bhaktitaḥ praṇamāmyaham ।। 

śrī mañjuśrīstavastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no mañjuvajrastotram

mañjugarbhakṛtam namaḥ śrīmañjuvajrāya

śaśadharamiva śubhraṃ khaḍgapustākapāṇiṃ suruciramaliśāntaṃ pañcacīraṃ kumāram ।
pṛthutaravaramokṣaṃ padmapatrāyatākṣaṃ kumatidahanadakṣaṃ mañjughoṣaṃ namāmi ।। 

kṛtamṛgaripuyānaṃ dattabhaktapradānaṃ suradanujanṛyānaṃ bodhisattvapradhānam ।
akhilaguṇanidhānaṃ sarvavidyāvitānaṃ karasarasijabāṇaṃ mañjughoṣaṃ namāmi ।। 

vibhṛtasakalakoṣaṃ kṣālitājñānadoṣaṃ smaraṇabhajanatoṣaṃ dūrarāgādidoṣam ।
vihitasasurapoṣaṃ siddhidākhyānayoṣaṃ kṛtajaḍapariśoṣaṃ mañjughoṣaṃ namāmi ।। 

gaṇapatiśarajanmaśrīmahākālasiṃhaiḥ parivṛtamiva candrābhābhamindīvarākṣam ।
asiśarajapamālāpustakaṃ saṃvahantam urasi lalitamālaṃ mañjughoṣaṃ namāmi ।। 

surapatiśamanāyāpyeṣa mitrāgnirakṣaḥpavanapramathapālaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ smeravaktram ।
khagapatirathagātraṃ brahmavandyaṃ ramomāvihitacaraṇabhaktaṃ mañjughoṣaṃ namāmi ।। 

yadasikaṭhinadhārācchedamārgābhivāhā sakalasaliladhārāpātitāṅgāṅgamantraḥ ।
bahuparicayasthalyāṃ bhūminadyāpi reje bahutaramahimānaṃ mañjughoṣaṃ namāmi ।। 

bhavadabhinavanutyā toṣitā guhyadevī nikhilanigamasārā suprakāśā atireje ।
bhavajalanidhipāraṃ dānakalpadrumāgraṃ galitabahumahograṃ mañjughoṣaṃ namāmi ।। 

vibhajati janaloko dharmadhātuṃ maheśaṃ daśaśatadalapadme saṃsthitaṃ jyotiraiśam ।
tadapi tava praśastaṃ devamāhātmyamīśaṃ vibhajati bhujageśaṃ mañjughoṣaṃ namāmi ।। 

paṭhati yadidamiṣṭaṃ mālinīpadyabandhaṃ sa bhavati kavirājo vādisiṃhāsanasthaḥ ।
sakalavisabhāsu projjvaladvāksudhāraḥ kalitasakalavidyo bhūṣaṇo bhavyadakṣaḥ ।। 

svayambhūpurāṇoddhṛtaṃ mañjugarbhaviracittaṃ mañjuvajrastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no māravijayastotram

jitamārakaliṃ jagadekaguruṃ surayakṣamahoragadaityanatam ।
catusatyasudeśitamārgamimaṃ guṇameghamahaṃ praṇamāmi sadā ।। 

bhavabhīmamahodadhimadhyagataṃ kṛpaṇārtaravaṃ samavekṣya janam ।
parimocayituṃ ya iha praṇidhiṃ pracakāra vibhuṃ tamahaṃ praṇataḥ ।। 

girirājanibhaṃ śaradindudhiyaṃ sumukhaṃ subhujaṃ vararūpadharam ।
sugataṃ gatamapratimaṃ sugataṃ praṇato asmi sadā jagadarthakaram ।। 

kanakaprabhayā paripītatanuṃ varadundubhitoyadavalgurutam ।
gajahaṃsavilambitadhīragataṃ śirasā abhinato asmi guṇaikanidhim ।। 

taruṇārkasamairacalairnayanaiḥ sphuradugramahāśanibhīmaravaiḥ ।
namucipraharairasiśaktidharaiścalito asi vibho na hi tvaṃ vikṛtaiḥ ।। 

lavalīphalapāṇḍurakarṇapuṭāḥ kucabhāravināmitagātralatāḥ ।
nahi tvāmaśakan khalu nāgasutāḥ śvasitaiḥ skhalitairapi kampayitum ।। 

taravaḥ kusumastabakābharaṇā bahuratnasahasracitāśca nagāḥ ।
na tathābhiratiṃ janayanti satāṃ janayanti yathā tava vīraguṇāḥ ।। 

sphuṭacitrapadaṃ bahuyuktiyutaṃ gamakaṃ vacanaṃ tava karṇasukham ।
śubhamārgaphalaṃ prasamīkṣyajanā na gṛṇanti punastvadṛte anyavacaḥ ।। 

iti vaḥ śaraṇaṃ samavekṣya janā na patantyapi kalpaśatairniraye ।
vinihatya ca doṣaripūn bahulān pariyanti śubhaṃ varamokṣapuram ।। 

tava saumyatayā apyabhibhūtatamo na virājati śītakaro gagane ।
tava kāñcanakuṅkumasaprabhayā prabhayā abhihato na vibhāti raviḥ ।। 

tava nātha śubhe vadanāmburūhe nayanabhramarā nipatanti nṛṇām ।
pratibuddhadale kamale vimale bhramarā iva puṣpaśatākulitāḥ ।। 

iti toṭakamantravarairatulaiḥ parikīrtya mayā tava varṇalavān ।
yadupārjitamadya śubhaṃ vipulaṃ śivamastu tato bhuvi devanṛṇām ।। 

śrīmāravijayastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no nairātmāṣṭakastotram

nirālambanirākāranirvikalpasvarūpiṇī ।
nairātmā varadā devī nityameva namo astu te ।। 

ekavaktrāṃ trinetrāṃ ca ūrdhvapiṅgalamūrdhajām ।
kare kartikapālāṃ ca namāmi viśvamātarīm ।। 

navanṛtyabhūṣitāṃ ca sahasramukharūpiṇīm ।
yogeśvarīṃ yogagamyāṃ namāmi jñānarūpiṇīm ।। 

śavārūḍhāṃ mahātejāṃ sarvaduṣṭanikṛntanīm ।
sarvapāpaharāṃ devīṃ namāmi jagadīśvarīm ।। 

gaurīṃ caurīṃ ca vetālīṃ ghasmarīṃ pukkasīṃ tathā ।
śabarīṃ cāṇḍālīṃ ḍombīṃ namāmi cāṣṭayoginīm ।। 

brahmāviṣṇuśivaśakracaturmāravināśinīm ।
trailokyamohinīṃ devīṃ namāmi surasundarīm ।। 

akṣamālavibhūṣāṅgīm akārabījasambhavām ।
nityaṃ dhyānaratāṃ devīṃ namāmi viśvamātarīm ।। 

sarvabhūtapriyāṃ devīṃ sarvamantraprabodhinīm ।
sarvamantramayīṃ mātarnairātmāṃ tvāṃ namāmyaham ।। 

nairātmāṣṭakastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no narakoddhārastotram

dāridrayapaṅkasaṃmagnaṃ saṃsārākhyamahodadhau ।
pratijñātaṃ samutpāde trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

timirāgārasaṃviṣṭamanarthaduḥkhavedinam ।
bandhuvargaiḥ parityaktaṃ trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

mātāpitṛbhaginyādi putradārasuhṛjjanāḥ ।
indrajālasamā dṛṣṭāstrāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

mayā arijanasyārthe sukṛtaṃ karma duṣkṛtam ।
ekākī taṃ hi bhokṣyāmi trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

jīrṇakūpe mahāghore anavagāhasāgare ।
andhībhūto asmyahaṃ nātha trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

jīrṇanauikāsamārūḍho mahāsāgaralaṃghane ।
durlaṅghyaṃ ca mayā dṛṣṭaṃ trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

dharmādharma na vijñātaṃ gamyāgamyaṃ na veditam ।
acetano asmyahaṃ nātha trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

mātṛghātādikaṃ pañcānantaryaṃ vā mayā kṛtam ।
pacyāmi narake ghore trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

kṛtaṃ mayā stūpabhedaṃ saṃghakāryaṃ vināśitam ।
kṛtā mayā sattvahiṃsā trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

ihaloke sukhairhīnaṃ paraloke na vedanam ।
veṣṭitaṃ karmasūtreṇa trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

kāśapuṣpaṃ yathākāśe bhramate vāyunā hatam ।
īdṛśaṃ jīvitaṃ loke trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

aṭavī kaṃṭakācchannā bahuvṛkṣasamākulā ।
panthānaṃ nātra paśyāmi trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

anaparādhāḥ kupitena mayā akāṇḍe hatā mṛgāḥ ।
rājahatyāṃ tadā manye trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

narake pacyamānasya kaścit trātā bhaviṣyati ।
gacchāmi śaraṇaṃ kasya trāhi māṃ hi tathāgata ।। 

vaidyānāṃ vaidyarājastvaṃ sarvavyādhicikitsakaḥ ।
lokanātha bhavatrātā trailokye sacarācare ।। 

narakoddhārastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no niraupamyastavaḥ

niraupamya namastubhyaṃ niḥsvabhāvārthavādine ।
yastvaṃ dṛṣṭivipannasya lokasyaiva hitodyataḥ ।। 

na ca nāma tvayā kiñcid dṛṣṭaṃ bauddhena cakṣuṣā ।
anuttarā ca te nātha dṛṣṭistattvārthadarśinī ।। 

na boddhā na ca boddhavyamastīha paramārthataḥ ।
aho paramadurbodhāṃ dharmatāṃ buddhavānasi ।। 

na tvayotpāditaḥ kaścid dharmo nāpi nirodhitaḥ ।
samatādarśanenaiva prāptaṃ padamanuttamam ।। 

na saṃsārātprakarṣeṇa tvayā nirvāṇamīpsitam ।
śāntiste adhigatā nātha saṃsārānaparādhitaḥ ।। 

tvaṃ vivedaikarasatāṃ saṃkleśavyavadānayoḥ ।
dharmadhātvavinirbhedād viśuddhaścāsi sarvataḥ ।। 

nodāhṛtaṃ tvayā kiñcidekamapyakṣaraṃ vibho ।
kṛtsnaśca vaineyajano dharmavarṣeṇa tarpitaḥ ।। 

na te asti saktiḥ skandheṣu na dhātvāyataneṣu ca ।
ākāśasamacittastvaṃ sarvadharmeṣu niśritaḥ ।। 

sattvasaṃjñā ca te nātha sarvathā na pravartate ।
duḥkhārteṣu ca sattveṣu tvamatīva kṛpātmakaḥ ।। 

sukhaduḥkhātmanairātmyanityānityādiṣu prabho ।
iti nānāvikalpeṣu buddhistava na sajjate ।। 

na gatirnāgatiḥ kāciddharmāṇāmiti te mati ।
na kvacidrāśitaḥ prokto dharmārthaparamārthavit ।। 

sarvatrānugataścāsi na ca yāto asi kutracit ।
janmadharmaśarīrābhyāmacintyastvaṃ mahāmune ।। 

ekatvānyatvarahitaṃ pratiśrutkopamaṃ jagat ।
saṃkrāntināśāya gataṃ buddhavān tvamanindita ।। 

śāśvatocchedarahitaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitam ।
saṃsāramavabuddhastvaṃ svapnamāyādivat prabho ।। 

vāsanāmūlaparyantakleśanadyo vinirjitāḥ ।
kleśaprakṛtitaścaiva tvayāmṛtamupārjitam ।। 

alakṣaṇaṃ tvayā dhīraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ rūpamarūpavat ।
lakṣaṇojjvalagātraśca dṛśyase rūpagocare ।। 

na ca rūpeṇa dṛṣṭena dṛṣṭa ityabhidhīyase ।
dharmadṛṣṭyā sudṛṣṭo asi dharmatā na ca dṛśyate ।। 

śauṣīryo nāsti te kāyo māṃsāsthirudhiro na ca ।
indrāyudhamiva kāyaṃ vinā darśitavānasi ।। 

nāmayo nāśuciḥ kāye kṣuttṛṣṇāsambhavo na ca ।
tvayā lokānuvṛttyarthaṃ darśitā laukikī kriyā ।। 

karmāvaraṇadoṣaśca sarvathā anagha nāsti te ।
tvayā lokānukampāyai karmaplotiḥ pradarśitā ।। 

dharmadhātorasaṃbhedād yānabhedo asti na prabho ।
yānatritayamākhyātaṃ tvayā sattvāvatārataḥ ।। 

nityo dhruvaḥ śivaḥ kāyastava dharmamayo jina ।
vineyajanahetośca darśitā nirvṛtistvayā ।। 

lokadhātuṣvasaṃkhyeṣu tvadbhaktaiḥ punarīkṣase ।
cyutijanmābhisaṃbodhicakranirvṛtilālasaiḥ ।। 

na te asti manyanā nātha na vikalpo na ceñjanā ।
anābhogena te loke buddhakṛtyaṃ pravartate ।। 

iti sugatamacintyamaprameyaṃ guṇakusumairavakīrya mayā prāptam ।
kuśalamiha bhavantu tena sattvāḥ paramagabhīramunīndradharmabhājanāḥ ।। 

niraupamyastavaḥ samāptaḥ ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no pañcākṣarastotram

namo buddhāya na jāto na mṛtaścaiva na rūpo nāpi rūpavān ।
na saṃsāre na nirvāṇe na kārastena sūcyate ।। 

mohadhvaṃsakaro nityaṃ mokṣasaukhyapradāyakaḥ ।
mohanaṃ sarvamārāṇāṃ mokārastena sūcyate ।। 

buddhānāmuditaṃ dhyānaṃ buddhānāṃ janamelakam ।
buddhaniḥkleśa saṃbuddha bukārastena sūcyate ।। 

dhāryate bodhisattvaiḥ sa dharmadhātugatiḥ sadā ।
dharmāṇāṃ paramo dharmaḥ dhakārastena sūcyate ।। 

yathā nāsti tathā nāsti yathā nāsti tathāsti yaḥ ।
yathāvādī tathākārḥ yakārastena sūcyate ।। 

pañcākṣaramidaṃ puṇyaṃ pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam ।
ye paṭhanti divārātrau te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

śrī pañcākṣarastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no pañcarakṣādevīstotrāṇi

mahāpratisarāstotram

om namaḥ śrīmahāpratisarāyai

tathāgatādyāstathatāṃ tattvamāpurmahattaram ।
dhāraṇīdhāraṇādyasyāḥ pratisarāṃ namāmi tām ।। 

raṇe śakro ajayaddaityān dhāraṇīdhvajadhṛg bahūn ।
saṃgrāmajayadāṃ bhīmāṃ pratisarāṃ namāmi tām ।। 

yatprabhāvād brahmadatto alabhad rājyamakaṇṭakam ।
sārvabhaumapradāṃ devīṃ pratisarāṃ namāmi tām ।। 

bahvaparādho api yadbhakto rājyādhikāramāptavān ।
śastrādibhītisaṃhatrīṃ pratisarāṃ namāmi tām ।। 

ratnānyavāpurvaṇijo yāṃ smṛtvodadhinirgatāḥ ।
sarvabādhāpraśamanīṃ pratisarāṃ namāmi tām ।। 

śrīmahāpratisarārakṣādevīstotraṃ samāptam ।

mahāmantrānusāriṇīstotram

om namaḥ śrīmahāmantrānusāriṇyai

buddhādhiṣṭhānato buddhābhayadāṃ bhayanāśinīm ।
bhavāmbudhinimagnānāṃ namo mantrānusāriṇīm ।। 

yanmantroccāraṇādeva ṣaḍītayaḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।
nāśaṃ prayānti varadāṃ namo mantrāmusāriṇīm ।। 

mantrānusāriṇo lokān nānye mantrādayo grahāḥ ।
pīḍayanti priyāṃścāpi namo mantrānusāriṇīm ।। 

buddho abhyabhāṣad gāthāstā yanmantrakathanāntaram ।
yābhiḥ sarvatra svasti syānnamo mantrānusāriṇīm ।। 

kalau buddhavihīne asmin lokānāṃ hitamācaret ।
pāpotpātapraśamanīṃ namo mantrānusāriṇīm ।। 

śrīmahāmantrānusāriṇīstotraṃ samāptam ।

mahāmāyūrīstotram

om namaḥ śrīmahāmāyūrīryai

duṣṭaṃ kṛṣṇabhujaṅgaṃ ca naraḥ svāntikaṃ pālayet ।
yasyā mantrānubhāvena māyūrīṃ praṇamāmi tām ।। 

brahmādayo lokapālā yaddhāraṇyā samāpnuvan ।
svāni svānyadhikārāṇi māyūrīṃ praṇamāmi tām ।। 

svarṇāvabhāsaṃ śikhinaṃ nālabhajjapinaṃ kudhīḥ ।
amoghenāpi pāśena māyūrīṃ praṇamāmi tām ।। 

yanmantrajapato jīvāḥ prājīvañchuṣkapādapāḥ ।
mṛtasaṃjīvinīṃ devīṃ māyūrīṃ praṇamāmi tām ।। 

yanmantrisaṅgāt pavano mahopadravaśāntikṛt ।
buddhānāṃ bodhidāṃ nityaṃ māyūrīṃ praṇamāmi tām ।। 

śrīmahāmāyūrīrakṣādevīstotraṃ samāptam ।

mahāśītavatīrakṣādevīstotram

om namo mahāśītavatyai

yaddhāraṇīmanujapan rāhulo bhadramāptavān ।
viheṭhito grahaiḥ sarvaiḥ śītavatīṃ namāmyaham ।। 

pāpatāpe śītakarīṃ śītalādyupasargataḥ ।
śītoṣṇaduḥkhaśamanīṃ śītavatīṃ namāmyaham ।। 

mantragranthitasūtrāṇāṃ dhāraṇāllakṣayojanam ।
pathikānāṃ pālayitrīṃ śītavatīṃ namāmyaham ।। 

śmaśānasthena muninā yā samuccāritā purā ।
grahopadravaśāntyarthaṃ śītavatīṃ namāmyaham ।। 

grahābhibhūtavātānāṃ granthipadavidhāriṇām ।
grahabhītipraśamanīṃ śītavatīṃ namāmyaham ।। 

śrī mahāśītavatīrakṣādevīstotraṃ samāptam ।

mahāsāhasrapramardinīstotram

om namaḥ śrīmahāsāhasrapramardinye

mahāsāhasrike loke sāhasrahitakāriṇām ।
sahasrasattvajananīṃ naumi sāhasramardinīm ।। 

sopadravāyāṃ vaiśālyāṃ mahotsavo yataḥ sadā ।
mahopasargaśamanīṃ naumi sāhasramardinīm ।। 

yakṣarākṣasabhūtānāṃ damanīṃ duṣṭacetasām ।
duritopadravahatāṃ naumi sāhasramardinīm ।। 

yaddhāraṇīpaṭhanato rakṣitaḥ śākyakeśarī ।
viṣato viṣadigdhāṃ tāṃ naumi sāhasramardinīm ।। 

madhumiśritabhaiṣajyaṃ sarvaroganivāraṇam ।
mṛtasañjīvanaṃ loke naumi sāhasramardinīm ।। 

śrīmahāsāhasramardinīrakṣādevīstotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no pañcatathāgatastotram

śrībuddha buddhādhipa buddharūpa buddhānvitān bodhayase vibuddhaḥ ।
buddhyā samastān khalu buddhaputra santoṣya yogena tu buddhameghām ।। 

śrīvajra vajrāmala jātavajra vajreṇa dīptena pradīpya lokam ।
dadan yogena tu vajrasaṃvarṣaṃ vajrātmabhāvaṃ kuruṣe suvajra ।। 

śrīratna ratnākara ratnamegha ratnena ratnaṃ ramase suratna ।
vidārya dāridrayaghanaṃ janānāṃ sutejasā ratnamahādhvajena ।। 

śrīpadma padmottama padmasattva padmānsamastān khalupadmajālaiḥ ।
vibodhya padmodbhava padmatoyaiḥ padme kule sthāpayase supadma ।। 

śrīviśva viśvāviśa viśvajñānaṃ viśvena viśvaviṣayena lipta ।
viśvena sattvān vinayeṣu viśvaṃ vidyāṃ suvidyḥṃ sukhapḥcitḥmiti ।। 

śrīpañcatathāgatastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no pañcatathāgatastutigāthā

om namaḥ śrīpañcabhūtāntāya ।

namaste varadarājāgra bhūtakoṭi namostu te ।
namaste śūnyatāgarbha buddhabodhi namo astu te ।। 

buddharāga namaste astu buddhakāma namo astu te ।
buddhaprīti namaste astu buddhamoda namo namaḥ ।। 

buddhasmita namastubhyaṃ buddhahāsa namo namaḥ ।
buddhavāca namaste astu buddhabhāva namo namaḥ ।। 

abhavodbhava namaste astu namaste buddhasaṃbhava ।
gaganodbhava namaste astu namaste jñānasaṃbhava ।। 

māyājāla namastubhyaṃ namaste buddhanāyaka । namaste sarvasarvebhyo jñānakāya namo astu te ।

śrī pañcatathāgatastutigāthā samāptā ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no paramārthastavaḥ

kathaṃ stoṣyāmi te nāthamanutpannamanālayam ।
lokopamāmatikrāntaṃ vākpathātītagocaram ।। 

tathāpi yādṛśo vā asi tathatārtheṣu gocaraḥ ।
lokaprajñaptimāgamya stoṣye ahaṃ bhaktito gurum ।। 

anutpannasvabhāvena utpādaste na vidyate ।
na gatirnāgatirnātha abhāvāya namo astu te ।। 

na bhāvo nāpyabhāvo asi nocchedo nāpi śāśvataḥ ।
na nityo nāpyanityastvamadvayāya namo astu te ।। 

na hyeko haritamāñjiṣṭho varṇaste nopalabhyate ।
na pītaḥ śuklaḥ kṛṣṇo vā avarṇāya namo astu te ।। 

na mahān nāpi hrasvo asi na dīrghaḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ ।
apramāṇagatiṃ prāpto apramāṇāya namo astu te ।। 

na dūre nāpi vāsanne nākāśe nāpi vā kṣitau ।
na saṃsāre na nirvāṇe asthitāya namo astu te ।। 

asthitaḥ sarvadharmeṣu dharmadhātugatiṃ gataḥ ।
parāṃ gambhīratāṃ prāpto gambhīrāya namo astu te ।। 

evaṃ stute stuto bhūyādathavā kiṃ vata stutaḥ ।
śūnyeṣu sarvadharmeṣu kaḥ stutaḥ kena vā stutaḥ ।। 

kastvāṃ śaknoti saṃstotumutpādavyayavarjitam ।
yasya nānto na madhyaṃ vā grāhyagrāho na vidyate ।। 

na gataṃ nāgataṃ stutvā sugataṃ gativarjitam ।
tena puṇyena loko ayaṃ vrajatāṃ saugatīṃ gatim ।। 

śrī paramārthastavaḥ samāptaḥ ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no pīṭhastavaḥ

brahmāṇī tattvarūpā vividhaghanaravā ghoracaṇḍī ca raudrī kaumārī kīrtikāmā pibati madhumadaṃ vaiṣṇavī gāyamānā ।
vārāhī vādayantī paṭutarapaṭahān nṛtyamānā tathaindrī cāmuṇḍā cāpi lakṣmīrharagaṇasahitā mātaro vaḥ punantu ।। 

gaṇapatiṃ ca herambaṃ vighnarājaṃ vināyakam ।
devaputraṃ mahāvīryaṃ mahābalaparākramam ।। 

mahodaraṃ mahākāyamekadantaṃ gajānanam ।
śvetavarṇaṃ mahādīptiṃ trinetraṃ gaṇanāyakam ।। 

akṣamālā varadaṃ dakṣiṇakarasaṃsthitam ।
paraśurmuṇḍapātraṃ ca vāmahastavidhāraṇam ।। 

nānāpuṣparataṃ devaṃ nānāgandhāvalepanam ।
nāgayajñopavītāṅgaṃ nānāvighnavināśanam ।। 

devāsuramanuṣyaiśca siddhagandharvakinnaraiḥ ।
pūjitaṃ vighnahantāraṃ mūṣakāṭaṃ namāmyaham ।। 

brahmāṇī brahmasāvitrī brahmatattvavivedinī ।
caturbhujā caturvaktrā caturdevaparāyaṇā ।। 

caturdeśe ciraṃ vyāpī caturyugopakāriṇī ।
haṃsayuktavimānasthā saumyarūpā pitāmahī ।। 

pustakaṃ puṣpamālāṃ ca varadābhayadhāriṇī ।
pītapuṣparatā devī pītāṅgā pītasannibhā ।। 

pītopahārasaṃyuktā pītagandhānulepinī ।
udumbaradrumasthā ca prayāgakṣetravāsinī ।। 

pūrvapīṭhe sthitā nityaṃ brahmaśaktirnamo astu te ।
māheśvarī mahādevī mohamāyāniraṃja nī ।। 

mahāvṛṣasamārūḍhā mahāhuṃkāranādinī ।
hemamukta nibhadehā kapālaśaśiśekharā ।। 

trilocanā triśulī ca akṣasūtrakamaṇḍalū ।
nānālaṅkārasarvāṅgī dakṣiṇena varapradā ।। 

sṛṣṭisthitivināśānāṃ sarvathāpīśvareśvarī ।
śvetapuṣparatā devī śvetagandhānulepinī ।। 

śvetavastraparīdhānā mudrābharaṇabhūṣitā ।
vārāṇasyāṃ mahākṣetre tāra vṛkṣanivāsinī ।। 

uttare saṃsthitā pīṭhe māheśvarī namo astu te ।
bālabhāve mahāraudrī kaumārī raktalocanī ।। 

raktavarṇadharā devī sindūrārūṇavigrahā ।
caturbhujā śaktisūtrasiddhapātradharā śubhā ।। 

kaumārī paramā śaktirmayūravaravāhinī ।
raktavastraparīdhānā raktamāṃsāvasāyinī ।। 

kolāpuramahākṣetre vaṭavṛkṣanivāsinī ।
agnipīṭhasthitā nityaṃ kaumārī te namo namaḥ ।। 

vaiṣṇavī viṣṇumāyā ca daityadurdāntanāśinī ।
haritaśyāmavarṇāṅgī garuḍopari saṃsthitā ।। 

śaṅkhacakragadāhastā caturbāhuvibhūṣitā ।
raktajvālā mahākrīḍā nānābharaṇabhūṣitā ।। 

haritapuṣpagandhā ca haritavastradhāriṇī ।
aṭṭahāse mahākṣetre kadambavṛkṣavāsinī ।। 

svarge martye ca pātāle sthitirūpeṇa saṃsthitā ।
tiṣṭhantī pīṭhanairṝtye nārāyaṇī namo astu te ।। 

vārāhī ghoraraktāṅgī raktakeśī mahodarī ।
daṃṣṭrāvādinī gambhīrā raktanetrā trilocanī ।। 

kapālamālikā mālā vicitrapuṣpaśobhitā ।
mahāśūkasamārūḍhā jvalitāgnisamaprabhā ।। 

aṅkuśakartikādaṇḍahāḍābharaṇabhūṣitā ।
trinetrā jvalitadehā ca duṣṭadarpavināśinī ।। 

jayantīkṣetrasaṃsthānā nimbavṛkṣasamāśritā ।
yāmyapīṭhe sthitā nityaṃ kolarūpī namo astu te ।। 

śakreśvarī sahasrākṣo kuṅkumāruṇavigrahā ।
sureśvarī devadevī sarvālaṅkārabhūṣitā ।। 

caturbhujā viśālākṣī chatraghaṇṭāvidhāraṇī ।
mahāvajradharā devī sthitā cairāvate gaje ।। 

nānāpuṣparatā devī nānāratnavibhūṣiṇī ।
nānāgandhaviliptāṅgī nānāvastravirājinī ।। 

cīra kṣetre mahākṣetre karañjavṛkṣasaṃsthitā ।
nāgapīṭhasthitā nityaṃ śakreśvari namo astu te ।। 

cāmuṇḍā caṇḍikā caṇḍī pracaṇḍasurasundarī ।
caṇḍāṭṭahāsā caṇḍākṣī pracaṇḍacaṇḍanāśinī ।। 

daṃṣṭrākarālā raktāṅgī kapilakeśī mahodarī ।
kṛṣā ṇī bhīṣaṇī raudrī jihvālalanabhīṣaṇā ।। 

mahāpretāsanārūḍhā bhujāṣṭakasuśobhinī ।
asicarmayutā hastaiḥ ḍamarukhaṭvāṅgadhāriṇī ।। 

kartikapālahastā ca varadābhayabhūṣitā ।
hāḍālaṅkārasarvāṅgī aripratyasudā priyā ।। 

sahasrasūryasaṃkāśā ropakūpaṃ prati prati ।
jvālāmālākulā dehe koṭisamaprabhā ।। 

bhūtavetālaḍākinyaḥ parivārāśca rākṣasāḥ ।
ekamakṣamahākṣetre aśvatthavṛkṣavāsinī ।
pīṭhe marutasaṃsthāne cāmuṇḍāyai namo astu te ।। 

mahālakṣmīrmahādevī bhogāḍhyā guṇasundarī ।
vaidūryapādukārūḍhā siṃhāsanasthitā sudhīḥ ।। 

caturbhujā viśālākṣī khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇo ।
pātrabindudharā devī hārdhayuk kuṇḍalī ।। 

ratnakhacitasarvāṅgī cūḍāmaṇivibhūṣitā ।
vicitrapuṣparatnā ca vastragandhānulepanā ।। 

trailokyavyāpinī devī sarvasthā sacarācarā ।
siddhagandharvanamitā vidyādharasurārcitā ।। 

devīkoṭamahākṣetre plakṣasaṃsthā varā balā ।
īśānapīṭhasaṃsthānā mahālakṣmīḥ namo astu te ।। 

jananī sarbabuddhānāṃ sarvasantoṣakāriṇī ।
tvameva sarvarūpā ca tvameva viśvarūpiṇī ।। 

bhairavaṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ raudraṃ ghoragambhorarūpiṇam ।
nirañjananibhaṃ dehaṃ sarvakāmamahotsavam ।। 

nānābhujasamākīrṇā nānāvastradharā śubhā ।
babhrurardhaśirorūhā dāvāgnisamatejasā ।। 

trilocanā mahātejā agnisūryasamaprabhā ।
triśūlaṃ muṇḍaṃ khaṭvāṅgaṃ ḍamaruṃ tarjanīṃ dhvajam ।। 

prajñāṃ tatpustakaṃ caiva khaḍgacarmadharā śubhā ।
pāśāṅkuśadharaṃ devaṃ vajrasūcīmahādharam ।। 

kapālakartikaṃ cakraṃ gajacarmāvaguṇṭhitam ।
daṃṣṭrākarālavadanaṃ vyāghracarmakaṭīvṛtam ।। 

sālaṅkāreṇa sarvāṅgaṃ narāsthipuṣpaśobhitam ।
śīrṣamālādharā devī kāpālikoṭaraṃ śubham ।। 

cūḍāmaṇiṃ mahātejaṃ kapālaṃ candrabhūṣitam ।
mahāpretāsanaṃ nityaṃ nīyamānā sadā priyā ।। 

sahasrasūryasaṃkāśā chatrabindusamanvitā ।
catuṣpīṭhasthitā nityam aṣṭakṣetranivāsinī ।। 

aṣṭamūrtisthitā devī aṣṭakayoginīpriyā ।
bhadrapīṭhe sthitā nityaṃ bhadrakālīsamāvṛtā ।। 

bhadrakāraṇakartā tvaṃ vīrabhadra namo astu te ।
asitāṅgo ruruścaiva caṇḍo atha krodhabhairavaḥ ।। 

unmattabhairavaścaiva kapālī bhīṣaṇastathā ।
saṃhārabhairavañcāṣṭabhairavāya namo astu te ।। 

svasthānā svādhikārā ca svasvarūpā svavīrakā ।
svasvacchavṛkṣatānaṃ na divyākṣaṃ caiva bhūmigāḥ ।। 

daśadikkṣetrapālaṃ ca kṣetrāṇi ca caturdaśa ।
pañcāśakṣetrapālaṃ ca kṣetrapāla namo astu te ।। 

nāthanātha mahānātha ādinātha mahāmate ।
śrīnātha siddhanātha mīnanātha namo astu te ।। 

kṣetranātha pīṭhanātha dvīpanātha mahātmane ।
pretanātha bhūtanātha baḍhanātha namo astu te ।। 

trināthaṃ navanāthaṃ ca ṣoḍaśanāthamuttamam ।
saptaviṃśatipañcāśacaturaśīti namo astu te ।। 

sarveṣāṃ nāthasiddhānāṃ mataṃ cakṣustvamavyayam ।
potasadma tathā vīrastataḥ sarva namo astu te ।। 

ekavāraṃ dvivāraṃ ca trivāraṃ yaḥ paṭhennaraḥ ।
śatamāvartayed yena prāpnoti phalamuttamam ।। 

nāśayecchokacintādi nāśayed vighnamaṇḍalam ।
nāśeyed rogakalahān nāśayed duḥkhaduṣkaram ।। 

nāśayed bhayadāridrayaṃ nāśayed ripujaṃ bhayam ।
nāśayedagnicaurādi nāśayed rājakopajam ।। 

nāśayed vigrahaṃ ghoraṃ parakṛtābhicārakam ।
nāśayed dveṣarāgādi nāśayet sarvapātakam ।। 

āyurārogyamaiśvaryadhanadhānyapravardhanam ।
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ yaśaḥsaubhāgyavardhanam ।। 

ṛddhiṃ siddhiṃ śriyaṃ lakṣmīṃ vidyāṃ jñānaṃ sutādi ca ।
buddhiṃ prajāṃ sumitrāṇi vardhayecca dine dine ।। 

nākāle maraṇaṃ caiva utpātaṃ nāśayet sadā ।
sarve rogāḥ praśāmyanti dīrghamāyuravāpyate ।। 

śrīpīṭhastavastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no potalakāṣṭakam

jaya siddhasurāsuralokaguruṃ kamalāsanasaṃsthitapādayugam ।
daśapāramitādikapadmadharaṃ praṇamāmi sadā varakāruṇikam ।। 

bahukoṭinarādhipalabdhavaraṃ jaya susthitasusthitanāthamunim ।
bhavasāgarapāragatādhikaraṃ śaraṇāgatasattvahitārthakaram ।। 

kamalāsanacārusurupadharaṃ amitābhatathāgatamaulidharam ।
kamalojjvalabhūṣitagātravaraṃ navabhāskaraśobhanadīptikaram ।। 

mṛdutāmranakhāṅguliśobhamukhaṃ śaśibimbasamaprabhasaumyamukham ।
ṣaḍabhijñaguṇākaravandyatanuṃ varasusthitanūpurahārayutam ।। 

maṇikuṇḍalamaṇḍitagaṇḍayugaṃ ghanagarjitatulyagabhīrarutam ।
girigahvaradyotanivāsakṛtaṃ vṛṣavāhanahaṃsamṛgāyuśatam ।। 

ṛṣidevagaṇādhipasaṃstutikaṃ jinarūpadharātmakabodhiparam ।
dvipadottamanāthasurādhipatiṃ bahusattvavimocanamuktikaram ।। 

dhvajachatrasuśobhitavāmakaraṃ malayāgiricandanadhūparatim ।
kamalotpalapāṭalidāmadharaṃ praṇamāmyatha pāṭalivṛddhikaram ।। 

jvararogavivarjitakuṣṭhaharaṃ bahubodhimanāghanabhadrakaram ।
navadurgatināśanamārgapradaṃ karuṇātathatādvayaviśvapatim ।। 

śrīāryāvalokiteśvarasya potalakāṣṭakaṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no prajñāpāramitāstotram lakṣā bhagavatīkṛtam

om namaḥ śrīprajñāpāramitāyai

nirvikalpe namastubhyaṃ prajñāpāramite amite ।
yā tvaṃ sarvānavadyāṅgi niravadyairnirīkṣyase ।। 

ākāśamiva nirlepāṃ niṣprapañcāṃ nirakṣarām ।
yastvāṃ paśyati bhāvena sa paśyati tathāgatam ।। 

tava cārye guṇāḍhyāyā buddhasya ca jagadguroḥ ।
na paśyantyantaraṃ santaścandracandrikayoriva ।। 

kṛpātmakāṃ prapadya tvāṃ buddhadharmapurassarām ।
sukhenāyānti māhātmyamatulaṃ bhaktavatsale ।। 

sakṛdapyāśaye śuddhe yastvāṃ vidhivadīkṣyate ।
tenāpi niyataṃ siddhiḥ prāpyate amoghadarśane ।। 

sarveṣāmapi vīrāṇāṃ parārthe niyatātmanām ।
vyāpikā jagatīmenāṃ mātā tvamasi vatsalā ।। 

ye buddhā lokaguravaḥ putrāstava kṛpālavaḥ ।
tena tvamasi kalyāṇi sarvasattvapitāmahī ।। 

sarvapāramitābhistvaṃ nirmalābhiraninditā ।
candralekheva tārābhiranuprotā asi sarvataḥ ।। 

vineyajanamāsādya tatra tatra tathāgataiḥ ।
bahurūpā tvamevaikā nānānāmabhirīkṣyase ।। 

prabhāṃ prāpyeva dīptāṃśoravaśyāyodavindavaḥ ।
tvāṃ prāpya pralayaṃ yānti doṣāvādāśca vādinām ।। 

tvameva trāsajananī bālānāṃ bhīmadarśanā ।
āśvāsajananī cāpi viduṣāṃ saumyadarśanā ।। 

yasya tvayyapyabhiṣvaṅgastvannāthasya na vidyate ।
tasyāmba! kathamanyatra rāgadveṣau bhaviṣyataḥ ।। 

nāgacchasi kutaścittvaṃ kutracinna ca gacchasi ।
sthāneṣvapi ca sarveṣu vidvadbhirnopalabhyase ।। 

ye tvāmeva na paśyanti prapadyante ca bhāvataḥ ।
prapadya ca vimucyante tadidaṃ mahadadbhutam ।। 

tvāmeva badhyate paśyannapaśyanna vibadhyate ।
tvāmeva mucyate paśyannapaśyanna vimucyate ।। 

aho vismayanīyāsi gambhīrāsi yaśasvinī ।
sudurbodhāsi māyeva dṛśyase na ca dṛśyase ।। 

buddhaiḥ pratyekabuddhaiśca śrāvakaiśca niṣevite ।
mārgastvameko mokṣasya nāstyanya iti niścayaḥ ।। 

vyavahāraṃ puraskṛtya prajñaptyartha śarīriṇām ।
kṛpayā lokanāthaistvamucyase ca na cocyase ।। 

śaktaḥ kastvāmiha stotuṃ nirnimittāṃ nirañjanām ।
sarveṣāṃ viṣayātītā yā tvaṃ kvacidaniśritā ।। 

satyevamapi saṃvṛtyā vākyārthairvayamīdṛśaiḥ ।
tvāmastutyāmapi stutvā tuṣṭuvantaḥ sunirvṛtāḥ ।। 

prajñāpāramitāṃ stutvā yanmayopacitaṃ śubham ।
tenāstvāśu jagat kṛtsnaṃ prajñāpāraparāyaṇam ।। 

śrīlakṣābhagavatī kṛtaṃ prajñāpāramitāstotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no prajñāpāramitāstutiḥ

om namaḥ śrīprajñāpāramitāyai

nirvikalpe nirālambe niravadye niraṃjane ।
nityānitye nirvikāre prajñe devi namo astu te ।। 

buddhānāṃ jananīśāni bodhisattvapitāmahi ।
prapitāmahi sattvānāṃ prajñe devi namo astu te ।। 

mātarmātarjaganmātariti saṃjapatāṃ nṛṇām ।
manorathaprade śuddhe prajñe devi namo astu te ।। 

lakṣmīstvamasi kalyāṇi śrīrdhīḥ śraddhā dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ ।
sarvasvarūpe sarveśi prajñe devi namo astu te ।। 

lokottare laukike ca prajñāpāramite amite ।
daśa pāramitākāre prajñe devi namo astu te ।। 

śrīprajñāpāramitāstutiḥ samāptā ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no pratisarāstotram

om namaḥ śrīpratisarāyai pratisarai!

amaraughaiḥ pūjitāṃ tvāṃ nato asmi pratipadajanarakṣākāriṇīṃ sarvakālam ।
bhṛgudahanasamudrāpātaduḥkhe surakṣāṃ ripuviṣabhayahatrīṃ rājyabhogādikartrīm ।। 

parivṛtanijavargān bhaktadattāpavargān kalitaduritavargān mokṣalābhaikamārgān ।
kṛtanarasurasargān kāritānaṅgabhaṅgān stutikṛtamunigargān sarvarakṣaikasaṅgān ।। 

prahṛtasakalavighne sarvalokaikamānye daśabalakṛtadhanye pañcadevīvareṇye ।
viṣamapadaśaraṇye sarvadā tvāṃ namasye vasita iva araṇye dāvadagdhe virasye ।। 

sakalajanasuvāñchāpūraṇe kāmadhenumabhilaṣitaphalāptyai kalpavṛkṣāgravallīm ।
asurasuranarādyairvanditāṅghryabjayugmāmurasi lalitānānāratnamālādiyuktām ।। 

uḍupatiśatadīptāṃ śaṅkhakundāvadātāṃ grahabhayapariśāntāṃ vajrasattvātmikāṃ tām ।
śravaṇalalitalole kuṇḍale saṃvahantīṃ mukuṭamaṇiśikhābhiḥ kāśitāṃ tāṃ namāmi ।। 

janani sakaladuḥkhāttāraṇī tvaṃ prasīda sapadi vigatarakṣāṃ rakṣa me mātaraṃ ca ।
sakaruṇaruditaṃ māṃ tvaddayāsvasthabhūtaṃ kṛtasarasinipātāṃ tvaṃ gatistvaṃ gatirnau ।। 

paṭhati pratisarāyāḥ stotrametatsadā yo jvalanajalaviṣāṇāṃ coraśārdūlakānām ।
sagadanidhanakānāṃ bhītayā nāśayantī pratipadamalabhagnaṃ kāmunā dhairyalābham ।। 

nijajanapariyuktā dharmakāmārthavṛddhā ripugaṇaparimuktā saukhyameva prabhuktā ।
dadati vipulabhogyaṃ kāmadā sarvadā asau nihatasakalapāpaṃ mokṣamāyānti cānte ।। 

vigalitanayanāmbuḥ sāñjaliḥ saṃvilāpī stutimiti pracakāra traibhavānāṃ jananyāḥ ।
bhavatu mama tu saṃpat sarvabhāvā kṛśāno tanu kuśalasurakṣā itthamevaṃ sucittaḥ ।। 

vipacatu mayi sarvaṃ mādṛśaṃ karma bhogyaṃ sasuranaracayānāṃ bhrātṛmātṛdruhāṇām ।
kuruta kuruta dhairyaṃ yena mokṣaṃ sulabhyaṃ jaṭharanilayavāsaṃ māstu pāpaṃ kadācit ।। 

udaranarakavāsaṃ ye tadā sāvatāraṃ satataśubhasucetāḥ sādhayiṣyāmi bodhim ।
kṛtajagati surakṣāṃ yena kaivalyaprāptiḥ iti muditasucetāḥ karmaṇā digdhacittaḥ ।। 

pratisara avatāryāṃ sāmbikāṃ mā vilamba aniśamitivadan so nindayan vai svakarma ।
pratibhayaviṣadigdhastasthivānarbhakaḥ san muhuriha hi śaraṇyāṃ tāṃ smaran sarvarakṣām ।। 

aho sudhanyā jagadekamātā prakrāntadaivā ripuvargabhītā ।
yasyāḥ prabhāvādvihitātyapāpāt prayāti vahnirjalaśītalatvam ।। 

prabhāvatāho punareva tasyāḥ vahniṃ jalaṃ cāpi giriṃ sthalaṃ vai ।
yasyāḥ smṛtenaiva savismatīyān vaiśvānaraḥ prāpa dvidhākṛtiṃ tām ।। 

gopāśarīraṃ hradapātaśītaṃ śaitaṃ tvanāśārthamivādhikoṣṇām ।
daivādidattābhijane samantānnitāntadūrādatipāpadattām ।। 

śrībhadrakalpāvadānoddhṛtaṃ yaśodharāgarbhasthabālakṛtaṃ pratisarāstotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no rakṣākāla stavaḥ

om namo lokanāthāya

mayā kṛtāni pāpāni kāyavākacittasaṃcayaiḥ ।
tatsarvaṃ hara me nātha rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

nepāle dvādaśābdeṣu anāvṛṣṭirmahābhayam ।
narendradevaṃ saṃsthāpya rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

martyabhūmau ca pātāle duḥkhino bahulaukikāḥ ।
sukhavṛddhikarasteṣāṃ rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

yatra yatra gatastatra sarvasattvānukampayā ।
samuddharasi pāpebhyo rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

saṃsāre vyāpito ahaṃ tu kathaṃ pāraṃ prayāsyate ।
tvameva śaraṇaṃ tatra rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

sarvadevamayastvaṃ hi sarvabuddhamayastathā ।
sarvasiddhimayaścaiva rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

sadā kṛpāmayastvaṃ hi sadā rakṣāmayo asi ca ।
sadā prajñāmayastvaṃ hi rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

yena yena kṛtaṃ karma tena tenaiva dhāritam ।
yadyadicchāṃ pradātāsi rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

sukhāvatīṃ na saṃprāptaṃ yāvaddhi sarvasattvakam ।
tāvatsaṃsāragarte asmin rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

jñānināṃ jñānarūpo asi duḥkhināṃ duḥkhahārakaḥ ।
kāmināṃ kāmarūpo asi rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

pūjanīyo asi lokeśa praṇavasya svarūpadhṛk ।
vandanīyaḥ sadā tvaṃ hi rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

bharti vā bhartiko vāpi mitraṃ vā śatruko api vā ।
sarvatra ca dayāyukto rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

lokanātha jagatsvāmin subhaktikṛtacetasā ।
tvāṃ namāmi punarbhūyo rakṣa māṃ lokanāyaka ।। 

anekaduḥkhabhāgasmi bhīṣmairvai kaṣṭasaṃkaṭaiḥ ।
dayasva cāvalokeśa mocayasva ca māṃ kṣaṇāt ।। 

sarvadekṣāsusampātaṃ vartayan kuru me akṣayam ।
astu te karuṇā mahyaṃ bhaktiṃ caivācalāṃ kuru ।। 

śrīmadāryāvalokiteśvarabhaṭṭārakasya rakṣākāla stavaḥ samāptaḥ ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no ratnamālāstotram

ācāryavanaratnapādaviracitam lokeśvaraṃ

vimalaśūnyakṛpārdracittaṃ mārgajñatāprathitadeśanayārthavācam ।
sarvajñatādiparipūrṇaviśuddhadehaṃ jñānādhikāralalitaṃ śirasā namāmi ।। 

vaineyabhedavaśato bahudhāvabhāsaireko api pātragajaleṣu śaśīva yasmāt ।
saṃlakṣase parahitānugataiva tasmād buddhistvaho paramavismayanīyarūpā ।। 

saṃpūrṇacandravadane lalito lalāṭadeśādvinirgatamaheśvaradevaputraḥ ।
vaineyaśāmbhavajanapratibodhanārthaṃ devādhidevapratimānuja īśvarastvam ।। 

vaineyakomalabhavapratibodhanāya kiṃ dhāma saṃbhṛta mahāśubhalakṣaṇaṃ te ।
niryāta eva hi pitāmahadevapūjāṃ lokeśvareśvaraparaṃ śirasā namāmi ।। 

vaineyavaiṣṇavajanapratibodhanāya rājīvapāṇihṛdayāt pratiniḥsṛto asau ।
nārāyaṇo api bhuvaneśvara eva tasmāt puṃsāṃ tvameva paramottama eva nānyaḥ ।। 

candrārkasādarabalāhitabhaktibhājāṃ saṃdarśanārthamibhanīlasulocanābhyām ।
yanniḥsṛtau śaśiravī bhuvi locanābhyāṃ dhvastāntarālatamasaṃ tamahaṃ namāmi ।। 

sārasvatīvinayayojitabhaktibhājāṃ bodhāya vai bhagavatīha sarasvatīyam ।
dṛṣṭāgratastava jinātmajapaprasūtā prajñābhilāṣiphaladaṃ tamahaṃ namāmi ।। 

vaineyavāyujanitākṣaramārgasiddhyai yo lokanātha sugato atha viniḥsṛto asau ।
devaḥ samīraṇavaro bhuvi janmabhājāmīryāpathārthaphaladaṃ tamahaṃ namāmi ।। 

vaineyavāruṇaśivāyanamīpsitānāṃ saṃbodhanārthamudarātsugatātmajānām ।
yanniḥsṛto varuṇadevavaro apyakasmādaiśvaryasiddhi phaladaṃ tamahaṃ namāmi ।। 

vaineyasaṃmataphalādyabhilāṣiṇo vai saṃsiddhaye pravaralakṣaṇapādapadme ।
yanniḥsṛtā bhagavatī dharaṇī prasiddhā trailokyanāthamasamaṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

saṃsāramuktamapi susthitameva tatra kāruṇyataśca bhavacāriṇi sattvavarge ।
bhūyāt sthitirmama sadāsthirasā bhavantamevaṃ mahāśayavaraṃ paramaṃ namāmi ।। 

ekena pādatalakena bhavatsvakena cakrāntasaṃvaramanantaralokadhātau ।
kalpāntadagdhabhuvane jvalitogravahnirniḥśvāsavāyubalatastava nirvṛtaḥ syāt ।। 

svāṃ tarjanīṃ mukhadhṛto ahitatarjanena saṃcālitāśca bahumerugaṇā nakhasya ।
koṣoddhṛtaṃ jaladhitoyamaśeṣataḥ syāt sāmarthyamīdṛśamaho bhavataḥ kuto anyat ।। 

kvedaṃ ca śaiśavaparaṃ nanu cārurupaṃ saṃdarśanīyavarakomalabālacandram ।
durvāramāramathanaṃ ca mayaikasahyaṃ vikrāntaduḥsahaparaṃ kva ca ceṣṭitaṃ te ।। 

eṣā batāñjananibhorujanāvalī sā kauṭilyacāruvikaṭā svaśiroruhāgre ।
kleśendhane jvalitavisphuritatvavahnerdhūmāvalīva vimalā nanu lakṣyate te ।। 

tvatkāntileśavimalā daśadikpratānaiḥ pakṣāsitakṣayakṛśā sakalā suśobhā ।
paryanta iṣṭaśaśino bhavaneṣu yatte manye virāji nikhilaṃ tava kāntileśāt ।। 

bandhurhi ko mārgikasaṃmataṃ mataṃ naro narī sā sa ca satpathaṃ patham ।
parārthasaṃpāditasaṃvaraṃ varaṃ namāmi bhūmīśvararājinaṃ jinam ।। 

anityanirvāṇapade sthitaṃ sthitaṃ prabhāsvarādhiṣṭhitasaṃhitaṃ hitam ।
śamīkṛtāśeṣajanaṃ śivaṃ śivaṃ namāmi bhūmīśvararājinaṃ jinam ।। 

gabhastimālāmitasaṃkulaṃ kulaṃ tatra svapāṇau dhṛtapaṅkajaṃ kajam ।
ratānugāśobhitasaṃrataṃ rataṃ namāmi bhūmīśvararājinaṃ jinam ।। 

svadharmadhātuṃ karuṇāparaṃ paraṃ śubhādisaṃbhārasusaṃbhṛtaṃ bhṛtam ।
vikalpahīnaṃ dhvanideśakaṃ śakaṃ namāmi bhūmīśvarājinaṃ jinam ।। 

tathatātathatādvayaśātaśataṃ sadasatparipūritadharmakatham ।
kathanīyavirājitasatyaparaṃ praṇame dharaṇīśvararājavaram ।। 

varavārijarūpi jagatprasaraṃ sarasīruhalocanacārutaram ।
tarasāpi rasatvaviśuddhiparaṃ praṇame dharaṇīścarājavaram ।। 

varanirmitabhogaparārtharataṃ rataśūnyanirañjanadharmadharam ।
dharaṇīndravibhūṣitasiddhiparaṃ praṇame dharaṇīśvararājavaram ।। 

varasatsahajodadhicandramukhaṃ sukhabhāṣitasattvavimuktipadam ।
padabhūṣaṇalakṣaṇatānuparaṃ praṇame dharaṇīśvararājavaram ।। 

lokeśvareyaṃ tava ratnamālāmacīkaracchrīvanaratnapādaḥ ।
avāpi yattena śubhapraviṣṭaṃ tenaiva loko astu samantabhadraḥ ।। 

śrīmadāryāvalokiteśvarabhaṭṭārakasya ratnamālāstotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no rūpastavaḥ

sarvabhūtamaṇikampita tubhyaṃ kṣāntimeva caritaṃ tava rūpam ।
sarvarūpavaradivyasurūpaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavararūpam ।। 

bhṛṅgarājaśikhimūrdhni sukeśaṃ kokilābhaśikhidivyasukeśam ।
snigdhanīlamṛdukuñcitakeśaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavarakeśam ।। 

śaṅkhakundakumudaṃ vimaromaṃ janmaduḥkhavigataṃ vimaromam ।
rogaśokavimate vimaromaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavararomam ।। 

pūrṇacandradyutiśobhitavaktraṃ tuṅganāsamaṇibhāśubhavaktram ।
buddhapaṅkajinabhāmaravaktraṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaravaktram ।। 

raśmisahasravicitrasumūrdhni puṣpavarṣaśatapūjitamūrdhni ।
ratnavarṣaśatapūjitamūrdhni taṃ namāmi daśabalavaramūrdhni ।। 

netrapatākavilambitaśīrṣaṃ kāñcanachatravaropitaśīrṣam ।
netravitānasuśobhitaśīrṣaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaraśīrṣam ।। 

divyāmbaramukuṭaṃ maṇimukuṭaṃ candraprabhāmukuṭāmaṇimukuṭam ।
āgataśīrṣamakhaṇḍitamukuṭaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaramukuṭam ।। 

cārudalāyatapaṅkajanetraṃ divyajñānavipulāyatanetram ।
dhyānamokṣaśubhasaṃskṛtanetraṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaranetram ।। 

śuddhakarṇaśubhaśuddhasukarṇaṃ śuddhaprajñavaraśobhitakarṇam ।
śuddhajñānavaraśuddhasukarṇaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavarakarṇam ।। 

śubhrakundaśaśipaṅkajadantaṃ tīkṣṇasulakṣaṇanirmaladantam ।
viśvapañcadaśapañcasudantaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaradantam ।। 

uccavākyasasurāsurajihvāṃ dharmajñānakṛtapāpadajihvām ।
gandhadhūpasasurāsurajihvāṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavarajihvām ।। 

meghasudundubhināditaghoṣaṃ satyadharmanayasuviditaghoṣam ।
divyavādiparavāditaghoṣaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaraghoṣam ।। 

grīvagrīvadaśagrīvasugrīvaṃ kṣāntivīryaṃ tava grīvasugrīvam ।
hemavarṇamaṇigrīvasugrīvaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaragrīvam ।। 

siṃhakāyahimakundasukāyaṃ dhyānakāyaguṇasāgarakāyam ।
aṣṭasulakṣaṇanirmalakāyaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavarakāyam ।। 

śvetaraktaśubhaśobhitavastraṃ nīlapītaharitāyitavastram ।
hāradhavalaśubhaśobhitavastraṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaravastram ।। 

hemanāgakarasaṃskṛtabāhū puṣpadānakṛtaśobhitabāhū ।
dhīravīryasumanoharabāhū taṃ namāmi daśabalavarabāhū ।। 

cāmaracakrasuśobhitahastaṃ vimalasukomalapaṅkajahastam ।
bhūtapretaśaraṇāgatahastaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavarahastam ।। 

rāgadveṣatanuvarjitacittaṃ kalpakoṭisamabhāvitacittam ।
śīlajñānasamabhāvitacittaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaracittam ।। 

padmanābhaśubhaśobhitanābhaṃ padmayoniśubhaśobhitanābham ।
brahmajyotisuśobhitanābhaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaranābham ।। 

cakrasulakṣaṇabhūṣitapādaṃ aṅkuśaśaktivirājitapādam ।
nāgayakṣagaṇavanditapādaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavarapādam ।। 

bhāskaradyutirājitapādaṃ devadānavagaṇavanditapādam ।
sarvadevagaṇavanditapādaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavarapādam ।। 

sarvadevagaṇapūjitaśīrṣaṃ sūryakoṭisamabhāvitaśīrṣam ।
divyajvālajvalitārpitaśīrṣaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaraśīrṣam ।। 

puṣpadhūpaśatapūjitaśīrṣaṃ dīpagandhaśatapūjitaśīrṣam ।
mālyavastraśatapūjitaśīrṣaṃ taṃ namāmi daśabalavaraśīrṣam ।। 

tribhuvanadharmakalābhyuṣṇīṣaratnachatramukuṭādipūjitam ।
ye paṭhanti sugatastavamenaṃ te labhanti śubhamokṣapathādhigamam ।। 

śrīmadāryāvalokiteśvarabhaṭṭārakasya rūpastavaṃ samāptam ।।

rūpalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇo hīnoccasamasevanaḥ ।
sandarśaya sadā dānaṃ namaste dānapāraga ।। 

śabdalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇaḥ suśobho guṇasāgaraḥ ।
saṃśrāvaya sadā śīlaṃ namaste śīlapāraga ।। 

gandhalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇo divyaprāṇo vināyakaḥ ।
saṃprāpaya jina kṣāntiṃ namaste kṣāntipāraga ।। 

rasalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇaḥ sujihvo dharmadeśakaḥ ।
bhāṣasva saugataṃ dharmaṃ namaste vīryapāragaḥ ।। 

sparśalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇaḥ aniruddho nirīhakaḥ ।
saṃsparśaya jina dhyānaṃ namaste dhyānapāraga ।। 

dharmalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇaḥ sattveṣu samacintakaḥ ।
prajñopāyamahāprāpta namaste buddhipāraga ।। 

ṣaḍabhijñastavaṃ yo ayaṃ trisandhyaṃ bhaktimān paṭhet ।
saṃsārabandhanaṃ hitvā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

śrīmahābuddhabhaṭṭārakasya ṣaḍabhijñastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no ṣaḍgatistotram

paṅkeruhasthāya padāmbujāya bandhūkapuṣpāruṇasundarāya ।
sarojahastāya jaṭādharāya namo astu tasmai karūṇāmayāya ।। 

kāputradeśodbhavamaṅgalāya jinendrarūpāya tathāgatāya ।
saṃsāraduḥkhārṇavapāragāya namo astu tasmai karūṇāmayāya ।। 

samantabhadrāya surārcitāya suvarṇagraiveyakabhūṣitāya ।
cūḍāmaṇiśīrṣadharāya tubhyaṃ namo astu tasmai karūṇāmayāya ।। 

saundaryasāndrāya vṛṣāsanāya bhaktārtihantre ca tathāgatāya ।
mahārharatnaiḥ parimaṇḍitāya namo astu tasmai karūṇāmayāya ।। 

satkaṇṭhakaṇṭhāya manoharāya trailokyasaṃpūjitasampadāya ।
kāruṇyasaṃpūrṇahṛdambujāya namo astu tasmai karūṇāmayāya ।। 

stotraṃ pracakre bhuvi śaṃkhakarma puṇyārthato yacchatarājadhīmān ।
ye ye paṭhiṣyanti narāḥ prayatnāt te te gatāḥ śrīsuraharmyaramyam ।। 

śrī āryāvalokiteśvarasya ṣaḍgatistotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no saptabuddhastotram

utpanno vandhumatyāṃ nṛpativarakule yo vipaśyītināmnā yasyāśītisahasrāṇyamaranaragurorāyurāsīd gatānām ।
yena prāptaṃ jinatvaṃ daśabalabalinā potalāvṛkṣamūle taṃ vande jñānavāri praṇamitasakalaṃ kleśavahniṃ jinendram ।। 

vaṃśe pṛthvīśvarāṇāṃ mahati puravare yaḥ prajāto arūṇākṣo varṣāṇāmāyurāsīt sakalaguṇanidheryasya saptāyutānām ।
saṃprāptā yena bodhiḥ parahitapaṭunā puṇḍarīkasya mūle taṃ vande jñānarāśiṃ śikhinamṛṣivaraṃ prāptasaṃsārapāram ।। 

yo jāto nopamāyāṃ suprathitayaśasāmanvaye pārthivānāmāyuḥ ṣaṣṭisahasrādabhavadurumateryasya saṃvatsarāṇām ।
jitvā kleśānaśeṣānamṛtamadhigataṃ yena śālasya mūle taṃ vande dharmarājaṃ bhuvanahitakaraṃ viśvabhūnāmadheyam ।। 

kṣemāvatyāṃ prajāto manujapatisame yo vaśī vipravaṃśe āyurvarṣāyutāni pravaraguṇanidheraṣṭacatvāri caiva ।
jainendraṃ yena labdhaṃ tribhavavadhakaraṃ jñānakhaḍgeśvareṇa vande ahaṃ siṃhakāyaṃ sugatamanupamaṃ kakupchandaṃ munīndram ।। 

śobhāvatyāṃ dvijānāṃ narapatimahite yo anvaye saṃprasūtas tasyāmāyuḥ sahasrāṇyatiśayavapuṣastriṃśadevaṃ babhūva ।
buddhatvaṃ yena ratnācalavaraguruṇaudumbare prāptamāsīd taṃ vande śāsitāraṃ kanakamunimṛṣiṃ dhvastamohāndhakāram ।। 

vārāṇasyāṃ kṛṣīśakṣitipatimahite vipravaṃśe abhijāto yasyāmāyuḥ sahasrāṇyatiśayamahitaṃ viṃśatirvatsarāṇām ।
yena nyagrodhamūle tribhavajalanidhiḥ poṣito divyagatyā taṃ vande vandanīyaṃ munivaramanaghaṃ kāśyapaṃ lokanātham ।। 

yo jātaḥ śrīviśāle kapilapuravare śākyarājendravaṃśe yasyāsīdāyurekaṃśatamiha śaradāṃ sarvalokaikabandhoḥ ।
nirgatyāśvatthamūle namucimapi satā anuttarā yena bodhis taṃ vande śākyasiṃhaṃ suranaranamitaṃ buddhamādityabandhum ।। 

jātiṃ vipretivaṃśe nṛpavaramahite ketumatyāṃ gṛhītvā buddhatvaṃ yena labdhamatiguṇanidhinā nāgavṛkṣasya mūle ।
aṣṭāvabdāyutāni kṣapitabhagavato bhāvi yasyāgramāyur vande maitreyanāthaṃ tuṣitapuravare bhāvinaṃ lokanātham ।। 

stutvā vai saptabuddhān sakalamupagatān saptasaptārkabhāso maitreyaṃ ca stuvan vai tuṣitapuragataṃ bhāvinaṃ lokanātham ।
yatpuṇyaṃ saṃprasūtaṃ śubhagatiphaladaṃ dehināmeva sarvaṃ chitvā saṃkleśapāśān munaya iva caran nirvṛtiṃ sa prayātu ।। 

śrīsaptabuddhastotraṃ samāptam ।।

jagadguruṃ suranaralokapūjitaṃ kṛpāpaṭuṃ parahitamokṣadeśakam ।
vipaśyinaṃ tribhavamahaughasāragaṃ namāmi taṃ sugatagatiṃ tathāgatam ।। 

anantapāre bhavasāgare asmin nimajyamānaṃ prasamīkṣya lokam ।
prakāśito yena hitāya dharmo namo astu tasmai śikhine jināya ।। 

vande viśvabhuvaṃ buddhaṃ candrārkādhikatejasam ।
sāgaraughamivāgāghaṃ jñānena vinayena ca ।। 

yasyenduraśmipratimairyaśobhiralaṃkṛtā bhāti vasundhareyam ।
audumbaraṃ puṣpamivādbhutaṃ taṃ vande kakupchandamahāmunīndram ।। 

visāriṇā vigatamalena cetasā virāgiṇā satatahitānukāriṇā ।
hataṃ tamo vigatamalena yena taṃ surārcitaṃ kanakamuniṃ namāmyaham ।। 

prataptacāmīkararaśmigauraṃ sahasrasūryādhikadīptatejasam ।
lokottamaṃ sarvajanābhivandyaṃ vandāmyahaṃ kāśyapanāmadheyam ।। 

vākyāṃśujālaiḥ pratibodhya lokaṃ sūryāśujālairiva padmaṣaṇḍam ।
yo nirvṛtaḥ śākyamunipradīpastasmaiḥ namaḥ paramakāruṇikāya śāstre ।। 

maitreyanāmā tuṣitālayastho yasyaikajanmāntaritā hi bodhiḥ ।
utpatsyate yaḥ sugataḥ pṛthivyāṃ sarvātmanā ahaṃ praṇato asmi tasmai ।। 

stutvā mayā saptajinānatītānanāgataṃ cāṣṭamabodhisattvam ।
yatpuṇyamāsāditaprameyaṃ nirāmayāstena bhavantu sattvāḥ ।।

namaḥ śrīlokanāthāya

amitaruciśiraḥsthaṃ padmapatrāyatākṣaṃ duritakṛtavināśaṃ mohamāyā ahitākṣam ।
karadhṛtakanakābjaṃ lokapālaikadakṣaṃ praṇamitaśirasā ahaṃ naumi taṃ lokanātham ।। 

aruṇavaruṇaśobhābodhivijñānahetuṃ maṇimayamukuṭaṃ saṃsārakāmbhodhisetum ।
kṛtamanasijanāśaṃ bodhisattvādiketuṃ praṇamitaśirasā ahaṃ naumi taṃ lokanātham ।।

namāmi sarvabhāvena yoginījālanāyakam ।।

caturo amṛtabhāṇḍāṃśca bodhicittena pūritān ।। 

pullīramalayodbhūtaṃ khaṇḍakapālasaṃvaram ।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no sattvārādhanagāthā ārya nāgārjunakṛtā

sattvārthameva mayi tiṣṭhati sattvaśraddhā nānyatra sā, hyahamaho adhigṛhītasattvaḥ ।
caryā adhamā karuṇayā rahitā bhaved yā saṃbhāvyate karuṇayaiva prahāṇamasyāḥ ।। 

sattveṣu yasya nitarāṃ karuṇāpravṛttirārādhakaḥ sa mama śāsanamarmavettā ।
śīlaṃ śrutiśca karuṇā ca sudhośca yasya nityaṃ sa eva sugatārcanakṛnnigadyate ।। 

kalyāṇakāramadhikṛtya gato asmi siddhiṃ sattvārthameva tanumeṣa samudvahāmi ।
naivaṃ kriyeta yadi sattvahitaṃ mayā ced vyarthaṃ karomi tanupoṣaṇamannapānaiḥ ।। 

sattvān hinasti manasāpi hi yaḥ sa kasmānmāmeva saṃśrayati yo mayi nirvyapekṣaḥ ।
pūjā tu sā bhavati sattvahitekṣaṇāpi pūjyasya yā manasi tuṣṭimupādadāti ।। 

hiṃsātmikā paraviheṭhanasambhavā vā pūjā na pūjyamanugacchati saṃskṛtāpi ।
dārāḥ sutāśca vibhavaśca mahattva rājyaṃ māṃsaṃ ca śoṇitavase nayate śarīram ।। 

yeṣāṃ priyatvamadhikṛtya mayojjhitaṃ yat yastān viheṭhayati tena viheṭhito aham ।
sattvopakāraparamā hi mamāgrapūjā sattvāpakāraparayā ca parābhavaḥ syāt ।। 

sattvān prāpya mayā kṛtāni kuśalānyārādhitāstāyinaḥ prāptāḥ pāramitāśca sattvasamiterevārthamātiṣṭhatā ।
sattvārthena samudyatena manasā mārasya bhagnaṃ balaṃ sattvaireva tathā tathā viracitaṃ yenāsmi buddhaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। 

kasmin vastuni siddhyatāmiha kṛpā maitrī ca kvālambatāṃ kvopekṣāmuditādivastuviṣayaḥ kasmin vimokṣādayaḥ ।
kasyārthe karuṇāpareṇa manasaḥ kṣāntiściraṃ bhāvitā na syurjanmani janma priyavidhau mitraṃ yadi prāṇinaḥ ।। 

sattvā eva gajādibhāvagatayo dattā mayā anekaśaḥ sattvā eva ca pātratāmupagataṃ deyaṃ mayā grāhitāḥ ।
sattvaireva vicitrabhāvagamanādasmatkṛpā vardhitā sattvāneva na pālayāmi yadi cet kasyārthamarthaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। 

saṃsāre vyasanābhighātabahule na syuryadi prāṇino janmāvartaviḍambanena yamalokaṃ prāpya sātmīkṛtāḥ ।
saṃsārāttaraṇaṃ ca saugatamidaṃ mahātmyamatyadbhutaṃ kasyārthena samīhitaṃ yadi na me sattvā bhaveyuḥ priyāḥ ।। 

yāvaccedaṃ jvalati jagataḥ śāsanaṃ śāsanaṃ me tāvat stheyaṃ parahitaparairātmavadbhirbhavadbhiḥ ।
śrutvā śrutvā mama viracitaṃ sattvahetorakhinnaiḥ khedaḥ kāryo na ca tanumimaṃ muktasāraṃ bhavadbhiḥ ।। 

samyaksambuddhabhāṣitā sattvārādhanagāthā samāptā ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no śākyasiṃhastotram brahmaṇā kṛtam

namaḥ śākyendrāya ।

namo astu lokādhipa śākyarāja saddharmapaṅkeruhabhāskarāya ।
kleśārivargābhihatāya tubhyaṃ saṃbodhidīpairhatamohajāla ।। 

brahmarṣirājarṣisurarṣisaṅghaiḥ prāptuṃ na yacchakyamanekaratnaiḥ ।
prāptaṃ tvayā jñānamanantadharmaṃ yenākariṣyaḥ sakalasya haityam ।। 

pravartitaṃ yena sudharmacakraṃ yasmin mahī sodadhiśailarājā ।
ānanditeva calitā hyajasraṃ namo astu tubhyaṃ tribhavādhipāya ।। 

yasmiṃśca vātāstriguṇena yuktā vavurnabhasto nipatanti vastrāḥ ।
vicitrapuṣpāṇi sugandhi vāri namo astu tubhyaṃ jagadekanātha ।। 

ananyajeyo namucirvariṣṭhaiḥ sainyairvṛtaḥ koṭiśatapramāṇaiḥ ।
jitaṃ tvayaikena nirāyudhena namo astu tubhyaṃ balavartanāya ।। 

yena trilokīṃ pratipālituṃ tanmāyāsukajjājvalayan prajātam ।
svabhāvato janmajarāntakāriṇe namo astu tubhyaṃ jagadekanātha ।। 

traidhātulokeṣu vikāsituṃ tāṃ saṃbodhicaryāmapavargasetum ।
tuṣitāyuto janma cakāra martye namo astu tubhyaṃ varabodhirāja ।। 

samyak pratijñāṃ pratikṛtya yena saṃpreṣyate mokṣapure janaughaḥ ।
tadarthamāyāsi ca martyaloke namo astu tubhyaṃ sumahatpratijña ।। 

yaścāṣṭakaṃ brahmakṛtaṃ supuṇyaṃ paṭhiṣyati śākyavarāgrataḥ sthaḥ ।
duḥkhaṃ mahāpāpabhayaṃ ca hitvā śrīśrīghane yāsyati pattane mudā ।। 

brahmaṇā kṛtaṃ śrīśākyasiṃhastotraṃ samāptam ।।

chando amṛtoddhṛtam

namāmi taṃ bhikṣugaṇairūpetaṃ tathāgatairvṛkṣatale niṣaṇṇam ।
anantarodīritalakṣmabhājau pādau yadīyāvupajātayastāḥ ।। 

śākyendravaṃśālalitāvataṃsamaṃśādhikābhaṃ kanakādhikābham ।
namāmi buddhaṃ hyupajātisiddhaṃ sarvārthasiddhākhyakumāravaryam ।। 

namāmi nityaṃ niravadyavṛttaṃ niraṃjanaṃ nirmaladeharūpam ।
niḥśeṣasattvoddharaṇaikacittaṃ candrānanaṃ śubhrapadāravindam ।। 

śauddhodaniṃ gautamipālanīyaṃ māyāsutaṃ mārajitaṃ mahāntam ।
maheśvarādyairmahanīyamūrtimameyamāhātmyamameyadharmam ।। 

bhavodadhestīrṇamanantapuṇyaṃ bhavādidevairabhivandyapādam ।
anantabhavyākṛtibhāvanīyaṃ taṃ naumi bhavyojjvalabhūṣitāṅgam ।। 

babhāṇa vaṃśasthaviro nṛpādhipo janān pratītyāhvayatātmajaṃ mama ।
kṛtāribhaṅgaṃ jinarājamīśvaraṃ gataṃ ṣaḍabdaṃ ca viyogabhāvayoḥ ।। 

bhajasva vaṃśasthaviraṃ munīśvaraṃ mahāvane vṛkṣatale śucisthale ।
jagaddhitaṃ yajjanana jarāntakaṃ jagajjananyā varadakṣapārśvajam ।। 

śākyendravaṃśodadhicandramudgataṃ śrīśākyasiṃhaṃ caturānanaiḥ stuvan ।
prāśiṣṭa brahmā caturānanaṃ svakaṃ caturguṇaṃ puṇyamavāptamityaho ।। 

daityendravaṃśāgnirasau janārdano dvābhyāṃ vidhāyāñjalimambujāsanam ।
doṣṇāmamaṃsaccaturaścaturbhujād dvaiguṇyamāptaṃ sukṛtaṃ mayeti ।। 

chando amṛtoddhṛtaṃ śrīśākyasiṃhastotraṃ samāptam ।।

om namaḥ śākyasiṃhāya

namaste śākyasiṃhāya dharmacakrapravartaka ।
traidhātukaṃ jagatsarvaṃ śodhayet sarvadurgatim ।। 

namaste vajroṣṇīṣāya dharmadhātusvabhāvaka ।
sarvasattvahitārthāya ātmatattvapradeśaka ।। 

namaste ratnoṣṇīṣāya samantāttattvabhāvanaiḥ ।
traidhātukaṃ sthitaṃ sarvamabhiṣekapradāyaka ।। 

namaste padmoṣṇīṣāya svabhāvapratyabhāṣaka ।
āśvāsayanyaḥ sattveṣu dharmāmṛtaṃ pravartayet ।। 

namaste viśvoṣṇīṣāya svabhāvakṛtamanusthita ।
viśvakarmakaro hyeṣa sattvānāṃ duḥkhaśāntaye ।। 

namaste tejoṣṇīṣāya traidhātukamabhāṣaka ।
sarvasattva upāyeṣu sattvadṛṣṭaṃ kariṣyate ।। 

namaste dhvajoṣṇīṣāya cintāmaṇidhvajādhara ।
dānena sarvasattvānāṃ sarvāśāparipūraka ।। 

namaste tṛṣṇoṣṇīṣāya kleśopakleśachedana ।
caturmārabalaṃ bhagnaṃ sattvānāṃ bodhiprāptaye ।। 

namaste chatroṣṇīṣāya ātapatraṃ suśobhanam ।
traidhātuka jagatsarvaṃ dharmarājatvaprāpakam ।। 

lāsyā mālā tathā gītā nṛtyā devīcatuṣṭayam ।
puṣpā dhūpā ca dīpā ca gandhādevī namo astu te ।। 

dvāramadhyasthitā ye ca aṃkuśapāśaphoṭakāḥ ।
śraddhābhāvavinirjñātaṃ dvārapāla namo astu te ।। 

vedikādau sthitā ye ca catasro dvārapālikāḥ ।
muditādau daśa sthitvā bodhisattva namostu te ।। 

brahmendrarudracandrārkā lokapālāścaturdiśam ।
agnī rākṣasavāyuśca bhūtādhipate namostu te ।। 

anena stotrarājena saṃsthito maṇḍalāgrataḥ ।
vajraghaṇṭāgharo mantrī idaṃ stotramudāharet ।। 

durgatipariśodhanoddhṛtaṃ śrīśākyasiṃhastotraṃ samāptam ।।

praṇamāmi jinaṃ sugataṃ satataṃ tapanīyahiraṇyaśarīracchavim ।
varacakravibhūṣitapāṇitalaṃ sasurāsuramānuṣapāpaharam ।। 

praṇamāmi munīndraguruṃ lalitaṃ satatākulanirjitamārabalam ।
daśapāramitāpratibodhakaraṃ caturrāryavibodhakaraṃ sukaram ।। 

praṇamāmi hitaṅkaradevanaraṃ sanarāmarapūjitadevavaram ।
amarādikaṣaḍgatihaityakaraṃ sajarājanimṛtyubhayādiharam ।। 

praṇamāmi sukhākarabodhibharaṃ svasukhaṃ pradadau karuṇāśayataḥ ।
paraduḥkhamasahya cakāra janurgatadoṣanirākulaśākyakule ।। 

praṇamāmi ca lokahitāya gṛhaṃ vijahau pitaraṃ ramaṇīsahitam ।
hayakaṇṭhakachandakadevavṛto mudito abhyagamat suvane vijane ।। 

praṇamāmi tapovanasubhramitaṃ pracakāra ca yastu maharṣigaṇān ।
caturāryakabrahmavihāraparān sugatasmaraṇaikatapovratikān ।। 

praṇamāmi mahādrumamūlavare sutṛṇāsanasaṃśritavajradharam ।
śatakoṭisumārabalāstraharaṃ śatasaṃkhyatathāgataputravṛtam ।। 

praṇamāmi ca mallikapañcaśatā vaṇijaḥ pratipālanameva kṛtāḥ ।
vaṇijārpitapañcasudhānayakaṃ śubhapāyasabhojanabhakṣakṛtam ।। 

praṇamāmi suvartitadharmavaraṃ mṛgadāvavane caturāsanake ।
vidhiśakrasurāsuralokavṛtaṃ suśarīramahojjvalasarvadiśam ।। 

gurunirmitakaṃ sugatastavakaṃ paṭhanaṃ kurute kila yo manujaḥ ।
graharogabhayaṃ nahi tasya sadā sa tu yāsyati mokṣapure supure ।। 

ādityādinavagrahakṛtaṃ śrīśākyasiṃhastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no śākyasiṃhastotram śaṅkarakṛtam

namāmi saugataṃ jinaṃ lasadvitānabhāsuraṃ sahasrasūryarociṣaṃ śaśāṅkakoṭinirmalam ।
saromakūpamaṇḍalād galatsusūkṣmatejasaṃ sahasranemicakritāṅaghripadmapāṇiśobhitam ।। 

bhajāmi lokanāyakaṃ saśokaroganāśakaṃ jarāvipadbhayāntakaṃ bhavārṇavapratārakam ।
prabuddhapaṅkajāsanaṃ vibuddhabodhikānanaṃ trilokalokabhāvanaṃ jagattrayaikapāvanam ।। 

namo astu pālabhuṃ jagaccakāra janma mānavaṃ viśuddhaśākyasāgare payonidhau śaśī yathā ।
kathāsudhāmayo adhunā vinodayiṣyate bhavān trijālamohatāmasaṃ vināśayiṣyase jvalan ।। 

sthitāya bodhimaṇḍape hitāya lokasaṃcaya jitāya mārasainyakaṃ śritāya sattṛṇāsanam ।
sujātaśākyabhūpateryutāya pāramārthakairvṛtāya bodhisaṃvarairnamo astu dharmarāja te ।। 

bhajāmi bhavyabhāvukaṃ bhavasya bhāvabhedakaṃ subodhivaibhavodbhavaṃ subhādrikaṃ śubhāṃśikam ।
bhavaughabhārabhedituṃ babhāra bodhibhārakaṃ subhadrabhānubhāsvaraṃ subhāvitaṃ śubhāvaham ।। 

jinendramūlamaṇḍape lasadvitānavistṛte sahasrakalpapādape prapūrṇavatpraśobhite ।
hiraṇyaratnavedikākuśāsanasthitaṃ vibhuṃ namāmi śākyasaugataṃ tathāgataṃ varaṃ sadā ।। 

paṭhanti ye jināgrato vinirmitaṃ hareṇa tat supañcapañcacāmaraṃ trikālameva maṅgalam ।
sukīrtidharmasaṃyutaṃ lasanti sapta vṛddhayo vrajanti te sukhāvatīṃ sukhena satsukhāvatīm ।। 

śaṅkarakṛtaṃ śrīśākyasiṃhastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no śākyasiṃhastotram surapatikṛtam

naubhi śrīśākyasiṃhaṃ sakalahitakaraṃ dharmarājaṃ maheśaṃ sarvajñaṃ jñānakāyaṃ trimalavirahitaṃ saugataṃ bodhirājam ।
dharmādhāraṃ munīndraṃ daśabalabalinaṃ śrīghanaṃ viśvarūpaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ lokanāthaṃ sakalabhayaharaṃ saṃsthitaṃ martyaloke ।। 

yastvaṃ dharmādhimeśaṃ sakalajinasutaiḥ saṃśritaḥ śvetaketurityākhyāṃ bodhihetustadanu ca tuṣitā cāgatā bodhirāja ।
maitreyaṃ sthāpayitvā pramuditamanasaṃ svāsane cābhiṣiñcya māyāgarbhe pavitre aśucimalarahite ratnavyūhe niveśa ।। 

garbhe sthitvā api yastvaṃ sakalahitakarīṃ dharmavyākhyāṃ karoṣi kāle mātuḥ sukakṣātsakalanijakaraiḥ kāśayat saṃprajātaḥ ।
lokācāraṃ ca kṛtvā vihitadaśavidhiṃ vai vivāhādi tattat tyaktvā sarvāṃśca rājyaṃ sakalajanahite nirgataṃ tvāṃ name aham ।। 

ūrṇākośācca yasya pratidinamasakṛt dakṣiṇāvartarociḥ prodyaddedīpyamānatribhuvanakuharadhvastamohāndhakāram ।
catvāriṃśatsudantodgalitakaracayairbhāpayannārakīyān proddhṛtvā svargaloke suratarukalite sthāpitā yena vande ।। 

yatpāṇī cakracihnāvabhimataphaladau dānapāraṃgatatvodyatkāntā bhūmidevī svagaṇaparivṛtā bhedayitvā avaniṃ tām ।
sthitvāgre pūjayitvā namucimabhigataṃ bhartsayitvā dviṣantaṃ sākṣībhūtā nilīnā praṇamitaśirasā tvāṃ name ahaṃ jinendram ।। 

yasyodgrīvasya cāgre vidhiharamadhuhṛllokasaṃsthaiḥ pravīṇair draṣṭuṃ naivābhiśaktyā kimu manujapure vāsitairmādṛśaiśca ।
brahmāṇḍaṃ laṅghayitvā taraṇiśaśadharau dyauśca nakṣatralokaṃ ūrdhvaṃ lokottarākhye nijabhuvanavare bhāsitaṃ tvāṃ name aham ।। 

yadvaktraṃ paṅkajābhaṃ suradanavasanākarṇikākesarāḍhyaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ jūmbhate asmin bhuvanagaṇavṛttaṃ saṃśritaṃ karṇikāvat ।
dṛṣṭvā saṃmūrcchito abhūnnamuciranucaraistrāsi sarvajñanātha kṛtvā kecitprayātāḥ śaraṇamabhimataṃ śrīghanaṃ tvāṃ name aham ।। 

saṃkhyājñānapravīṇāstribhuvanasadane paṇḍitā ye vasanti taiḥ sarvairmīlayitvā yadi tava mahimā varṇyate kalpakālam ।
pāraṃ gantuṃ samarthā nahi nikhilaguṇakṣīrasindhoḥ kathañcid ekākī kiṃ samarthāstadapi mama mano bodhanārthaṃ name tvām ।। 

paṭhyante stotrametatsurapatiracitaṃ sragdharāvṛttasaṃjñaṃ śakrādyā lokapālāḥ pratipadanucarāḥ saṃkariṣyanti rakṣām ।
saukhyaṃ bhuktveha loke tadanu surapateḥ kalpavṛkṣābhikīrṇe sthitvā gacchanti cānte sugatasutamahīṃ sarvalaukaikagamyām ।। 

surapatikṛtaṃ śrīśākyasiṃhastotraṃ samāptam ।।

om namaḥ sarvajñāya

name śrīghana tvāṃ sadābhāvabhakto bhavāmbhodhisetuṃ lasanmokṣahetum ।
tridhātuṃ vidhātuṃ surakṣāṃ virakṣāṃ sudakṣaṃ sukakṣāṃ sujātaṃ sudāntam ।। 

name dānaśīlakṣamādhyānavīryaṃ mahajjñānapāraṃgataṃ saugatatvam ।
caturbrahmavaihāralokoddharantaṃ catuḥsatyadharmopadeśaṃ suveśam ।। 

name bodhirājaṃ sugamye virājaṃsuramye vane devarājādigamyam ।
caturthāsanasthaṃ hitārthaṃ diśantaṃ kṛtānekasusthaṃ jagadrakṣaṇastham ।। 

caturmāralokaṃ mahadvīryavantaṃ jayantaṃ hasantaṃ trijālaṃ ca kālam ।
kṣamānaddhadehaṃ name muktagehaṃ trilokyaikanāthaṃ tathā śākyanātham ।। 

name mārasainyaṃ jitaṃ yena sarvaṃ nirastreṇa sāhāyyamuktena nūnam ।
kṣamāvarma maitrīdhanurdhāriṇā ca jagatpālituṃ bodhivṛkṣasthitena ।। 

name śītavyañjairlasaddehagehaṃ jane snehavantaṃ vane gehavantam ।
yutaṃ dvādhikaistriṃśakairlakṣaṇākhyairmahādurlabhaṃ traibhave lokapūjyam ।। 

name dharmameghāsthitaṃ supratiṣṭhaṃ kalau nāthahīne bhaveyaṃ sanāthaḥ ।
tathā pālituṃ svāṃ pratijñāṃ cakāra janiṃ śākyavaṃśe mahīpāvataṃse ।। 

name bhāgyato labhyate darśanaṃ te tathā bhāgyabhājo svayameti buddhiḥ ।
sthito dharmameghe kathaṃ darśanaṃ syād vihīnā na tatrābhigantuṃ praśaktāḥ ।। 

idānīṃ bhavatpādapadmotthitena rajaḥpuñjakena trilokaṃ pavitram ।
tathāsmācchirāṃsi pavitrāṇi satyaṃ cariṣyāmi bodhiṃ bhavacchāsanena ।। 

bhujaṅgaprayātaṃ kṛtaṃ mādhavena paṭhed yo jinasyāgratastho hi nityam ।
sadā maṅgalaṃ tasya gehe sudehe prasannāśca rakṣāṃ kariṣyanti buddhāḥ ।। 

trijālaṃ ca chitvā sukhāni prabhuktvā tathā dānaśīlādipāraṃgatāśca ।
mahābodhilabdhā jagatpālakṣodaṃ gamiṣyanti cānte sukhāvatyupākhyām ।। 

śrīśākyasiṃhasya viṣṇukṛtaṃ bhujaṅgaprayātastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no śākyasiṃhastotram yaśodharākṛtam

eṣo hi bhavatastāto janmamṛtyujarāntakaḥ ।
sarvārthasiddhanāmneti śākyasiṃho adhunā suta ।। 

yasya chāyāmupāśritya divyātisundaro bhaveḥ ।
dvātriṃśallakṣaṇadharaṃ pitaraṃ darśayādhunā ।। 

caturaśītisāhasraṃ strīṇāṃ vihāya nirmadaḥ ।
tapovanamagād yo asau vandayainaṃ maharddhikam ।। 

saptaratnāni rājyaṃ ca mahaiśvaryapadaṃ varam ।
hitvā pravrajito yo asau taṃ darśaya jagadgurum ।। 

māyākhyāyāḥ pitāmahyā yo ajanaddakṣakukṣitaḥ ।
lumbinyāmudayāt sūrya iva taṃ pitaraṃ nama ।। 

abhayāyāḥ kuleśvaryā yena pādāmbuje natam ।
traidhātukādhipaṃ devaṃ pitaraṃ tvaṃ sadā nama ।। 

viśvāmitramupādhyāyaṃ yo ayojayat susaṃvare ।
bālakrīḍābhiraktātmā tātamenaṃ sadā nama ।। 

jambūtarusamāsīnaṃ pañcarṣayo hatatviṣaḥ ।
nirmāninaḥ prābhajan yamenaṃ tātaṃ sadā nama ।। 

pitaraṃ bodhayitvā yo atyājayattu ṣaḍaṃśakam ।
dayākaraṃ jagadvandyaṃ janakaṃ praṇamātmaja ।। 

yo ajayaddevadattādīn māninaḥ sarvavit sudhīḥ ।
sarvaphalādidaṃ vijñaṃ sudhiyaṃ janakaṃ bhaja ।। 

yātrāyāmāturaṃ jīrṇaṃ mṛtaṃ dṛṣṭivivarjitam ।
svayaṃ vijño api papraccha sadā taṃ janakaṃ bhaja ।। 

kāmāgnirnāharadyasya cittaṃ pramadavāsinaḥ ।
nirañjanaṃ nirvikalpaṃ suta taṃ janakaṃ bhaja ।। 

kanakāśvaṃ samāruhya chandakena bahiryayau ।
deśānniśīthe tridaśaiḥ stūyamānaṃ mudā bhaja ।। 

hayaṃ nivartayāmāsa chandakaṃ ca tapovanāt ।
sukaṇṭhābharaṇaṃ dattvā bhaṇainaṃ vanacāriṇam ।। 

nairañjanāmupāsṛtya prākarod yastapovratam ।
jagaddhitārthaṃ ṣaḍvarṣamenaṃ bhaja tapaḥparam ।। 

bodhidrumasamāsīno jitvā māraṃ suduḥsaham ।
prālabhadbodhiratnaṃ yo darśayainaṃ tathāgatam ।। 

mṛgadāvasthitaḥ kāśyāṃ dharmacarkra pravartayan ।
brahmādibhirvṛto yo asau darśayainaṃ guruṃ suta ।। 

iti mātroditaṃ śrutvā rāhulaḥ so ativismitaḥ ।
praṇamya pitaraṃ paśyan mudamāpa smitānanaḥ ।। 

śrīśākyasiṃhastotraṃ yaśodharākṛtaṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no śāradāṣṭakastotram

śaṅkhendukundahimasannibhacārudehāṃ haṃsasthitāṃ kamalapatrasurocanīyām ।
divyāmbarābharaṇabhūṣitasaumyarūpāṃ śrīśāradāṃ bhagavatīṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

saṃsārasāgaramahodadhimagnasattvasantāriṇīṃ suranarārcitapādapadmām ।
hārārddhahāramaṇikuṇḍalamaṇḍitāṅgīṃ śrīśāradāṃ bhagavatīṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

yā bhāratīti kathitā jananī ca loke mohāndhakārabharabhagnakṛtāṃ janānām ।
saṃkīrtitā munibhirastasamastadoṣaiḥ śrīśāradāṃ bhagavatīṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

vīṇānuvādanaratāṃ sphaṭikākṣamālāsaṃdhāriṇīṃ kanakapustakadhāriṇīṃ ca ।
ratnaiḥ śubhaiḥ surucirāṃ kṛtahastapadmāṃ śrīśāradāṃ bhagavatīṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

pūjyā sadaiva jananī parivandanīyā devyā gaṇā manasi saṃparimodanīyāḥ ।
jīvārthinaḥ phalabhṛto guṇavarṇanā ca śrīśāradāṃ bhagavatīṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

natvā bhajejjagati yo jananīṃ prasiddhāṃ kuryātsadā bhagavatī kilapañcasaukhyam ।
saundaryarūpaguṇavittasubhogabhājaṃ śrī śāradāṃ bhagavatīṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

pūjopahāravalibhiḥ paripūjanīyā devyā gaṇādikamanojñasuvaktrapadmāḥ ।
yaiḥ pūjitā bhagavatī kila jāḍyahantrī śrīśāradāṃ bhagavatīṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

yasyāḥ prasādamavagamya sukhapradāyāstrailokyanāthauditārkasamaprabhaḥ syāt ।
dharmārthakāmaphaladāmatha mokṣadāṃ ca śrīśāradāṃ bhagavatīṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

śrīśāradāṣṭakastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no sragdharāpañcakastotram

vande ahaṃ tattvarūpaṃ tatavitatabhavaṃ bhavyahavyasvabhāvaṃ buddhānāmādibuddhaṃ kṛtavividhahitaṃ tejasāṃ sannidhānam ।
samyaksaṃbodhimūrti triguṇavilasitaṃ pañcajñānaikahetuṃ nairākāraṃ nirañjaṃ gaganavadaniśaṃ nirmalaṃ cittacaityam ।। 

jyotīrūpe tvadīye vinilayatapasā dānaśīlakṣamāsu vīryadhyānākhyaprajñodadhikṛtataraṇo māṇivṛnde sujātau ।
bodhiṃ prāpto asmi cāsmin sakalapūravare cākaniṣṭhe mahimni vande tvāṃ viśvarūpaṃ sphaṭikamaṇirivopāttanānāprabhedam ।। 

nānā vaidhyaṃ supūjyopakaraṇamaniśaṃ ḍhaukitaṃ sarvalokai kiṃ cāhaṃ ḍhaukayiṣye tvadanunayamanāstyaktarājyādidravyaḥ ।
jātau jātau ca jātau kṛtasukṛtacayaṃ kāyavāṅmānasaistaistatsarvaṃ ḍhaukayiṣye nijatanusahitaṃ saṃgṛhāṇa subuddhe ।। 

ekaṃ yugmaṃ tṛtīyaṃ yugalayugamatho pañcamaṃ ṣaṣṭhasaṃjñaṃ saptāṣṭau vai navākhyaṃ daśamamatha tathaikādaśaṃ dvādaśākhyam ।
trāyodaśyaṃ caturdaśyamatha śarakamaṭhaṃ caikataḥ saṃprasūtam ānantyaṃ svaṃ tadaivaṃ jagadakhilamabhūt tvāṃ name caikarūpam ।। 

eko vairocanākhyastadaparajino buddha akṣobhyasaṃjñaḥ ratnādyaḥ saṃbhavo asau tritaya amṛtaruksaṃjñakasturyasaṃkhyaḥ ।
pañcākhyo amoghasiddhistadanu ca jagati khyātasaṃkhyādyasaṃkhyā devā daityāśca martyā bhavadavayavajāḥ sarvadā ahaṃ nato asmi ।। 

śrīśākyasiṃhabuddhakṛtaṃ sragdharāpañcakaṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no suprabhātastotram śrīharṣadevabhūpativiracitam

stutamapi surasaṅghaiḥ siddhagandharvayakṣair divi bhuvi suvicitraiḥ stotravāgbhiryatīśaiḥ ।
ahamapi kṛtaśaktirnaumi saṃbuddhamāryaṃ nabhasi garuḍayāte kiṃ na yānti dvirephāḥ ।। 

kṣapitaduritapakṣaḥ kṣīṇaniḥśeṣadoṣo dravitakanakavarṇaḥ phullapadmāyatākṣaḥ ।
surucirapariveṣaḥ suprabhāmaṇḍalaśrīḥ daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

madanabalavijetuḥ kāpathocchedakartus tribhuvanahitakartuḥ strīlatājālahartuḥ ।
samasukhaphaladāturbhetturajñānaśailaṃ daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

asurasuranarāṇāṃ yo agrajanmāgradevaḥ sakalabhuvanadhātau lokasṛṣṭyaikaśabdaḥ ।
svapiti manujadhātā abjayoniḥ svayambhūr daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

udayagiritaṭastho vidrumacchedatāmras timiranikarahantā cakṣurekaṃ prajānām ।
ravirapi madalolaḥ sarvathā so api supto daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

dviradadaśanapāṇḍuḥ śītaraśmiḥ śaśāṅkas tilaka iva rajanyāḥ sarvacūḍāmaṇiryaḥ ।
avigatamadarāgaḥ sarvathā so api supto daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

prabalabhujacatuṣkaḥ ṣoḍaśārdhārdhavaktro japaniyamavidhijñaḥ sāmavedapravaktā ।
amalakamalayoniḥ so api brahmā prasupto daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

himagiriśikharasthaḥ sarpayajñopavītī tripuradahanadakṣo vyāghracarmottarīyaḥ ।
saha girivaraputryā so api suptastriśūlī daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

jvalitakuliśapāṇirdurjayo dānavānāṃ surapatirapi śacyā vibhrame mūḍhacetāḥ ।
aniśiniśiprasuptaḥ kāmapaṅke nimagno daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

kuvalayadalanīlaḥ puṇḍarīkāyatākṣaḥ suraripubalahantā viśvakṛdviśvarūpī ।
harirapi cirasupto garbhavāsairamukto daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

kapilajaṭakalāpo raktatāmrāruṇākṣaḥ paśupatiratikāle saṅgabhaṅgaikadakṣaḥ ।
smaraśaradalitāṅgaḥ so api supto hutāśo daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

humaśaśikumudābho madyapānāruṇākṣo dṛḍhakaṭhinabhujāṅgo lāṅgalī śaktihastaḥ ।
bala iha śayito asau revatīkaṇṭhalagno daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

gajamukhadaśanaikaḥ sarvato vighnahantā vigalitamadavāriḥ ṣaṭpadākīrṇagaṇḍaḥ ।
gaṇapatirapi supto vāruṇīpānamatto daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

atasikusumanīlo yasya śaktiḥ karāgre navakamalavapuṣmān ṣaṇmukhaḥ krauñcahantā ।
trinayanatanayo asau nityasuptaḥ kumāro daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

aśanavasanahīnā bhāvyamānā virūpā alamakhilavighātaiḥ pretavaddagdhadehāḥ ।
ubhayagativihīnāste api nagnāḥ prasuptā daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

ṛṣaya iha mahānto vatsabhṛgvaṅgirādyāḥ kratupulahavasiṣṭhā vyāsavālmīkigargāḥ ।
parayuvativilāsairmohitāste api suptāḥ daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

yamavaruṇakuberā yakṣadaityoragendrāḥ divi bhuvi gagane vā lokapālāstathānye ।
yuvatimadakaṭākṣairvīṃkṣitāste api suptā daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

bhavajalanidhimagnā mohajālāvṛtāṅgā manukapilakaṇādā bhrāmitā mūḍhacittāḥ ।
samasukhaparihīnā vāliśāste api suptā daśabala tava nityaṃ suprabhātaṃ prabhātam ।। 

ajñānanidrarajanītamasi prasuptā tṛṣṇāviśālaśayane viṣayopadhāne ।
kāle śubhāśubhaphalaṃ parikīryamāṇe jāgarti yaḥ satatameva namo astu tasmai ।। 

tīrtheṣu gokulaśatāni pibanti toyaṃ tṛptiṃ vrajanti na ca tatkṣayamabhyupaiti ।
tadvanmune kaviśatairapi saṃstutasya na kṣīyate guṇanidhirguṇasāgarasya ।। 

suprabhātaṃ tavaikasya jñānonmīlitacakṣuṣaḥ ।
ajñānatimirāndhānāṃ nityamastamito raviḥ ।। 

punaḥ prabhātaṃ punarutthito raviḥ punaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ punareva śarvarī ।
mṛtyurjarā janma tathaiva he mune gatāgataṃ mūḍhajano na buddhyate ।। 

suprabhātaṃ sunakṣatraṃ śriyā pratyabhinanditam ।
buddhaṃ dharmaṃ ca saṅghaṃ va praṇamāmi dine dine ।। 

stutvā lokaguruṃ mahāmunivaraṃ saddharmapuṇyodgamaṃ nirdvandvaṃ hatarāgadveṣatimiraṃ śāntendriyaṃ nispṛham ।
yatpuṇyaṃ samupārjitaṃ khalu mayā tenaiva loko akhilaṃ pratyūṣastutiharṣito daśabale śraddhāṃ parāṃ vindatām ।। 

śrīharṣadevabhūpativiracitaṃ daśabalasya suprabhātastotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no svayaṃbhūstavaḥ

namaste viśvarūpāya jyotīrūpāya te namaḥ ।
namaḥ svayaṃbhave nityaṃ jagaduddhārahetave ।। 

tvaṃ buddhastvaṃ ca dharmo daśabalatanayastvaṃ tathā bodhisattvastvaṃ bhikṣuḥ śrāvakastvaṃ kuliśavaradharastvaṃ tathā dharmadhātuḥ ।
tvaṃ brahmā tvaṃ ca viṣṇuḥ pramathagaṇapatistvaṃ mahendro yamastvaṃ tvaṃ pāśī tvaṃ dhaneśastvamanalapavanau nairṛtastvaṃ maheśaḥ ।। 

bhūtāḥ pretāścatiryak tvamamaramaditimārnavāstvaṃ vayaṃ ca cāturyonistvameva triguṇavaratanuḥ pañcajñānaikamūrtiḥ ।
varṇāstvaṃ kālamāsā dinamapi rajanī pañcabhūtāstvameva annaṃ ratnaṃ ca sarvaṃ matirati mahatī naḥ sadā tvāṃ natāḥ smaḥ ।। 

pañcajñānena buddhān sṛjasi svayamatho bodhisattvāṃśca pañcabhūtānetān guṇāṃstrīnajaharigiriśān sthāvarāñjaṅgamāṃśca ।
sarveṣāṃ cetasi stho naṭayasi sakalaṃ sarvato rakṣako asi tvaṃ bījaṃ cāṅkurastvaṃ phalamapi viṭapī sarvadā tvāṃ natāḥ smaḥ ।। 

śreṣṭhaṃ kṣatraṃ tvamasmin prabhavasi bhagavān sarvataḥ sarvadevān grāmāṃstīrthāni deśān nṛpasahitanarān naigamāṃścāpi sarvān ।
dvīpeṣvanyeṣvapi tvaṃ vibhajasi sakalaṃ jyotiṣāṃ saṃvibhāgam bījībhūtaikadīpo asyakhilamapi jagadvayāpakastvāṃ natāḥ smaḥ ।। 

jyotistvadīyaṃ parito visāri sitāruṇaśyāmakapītaraktaṃ ।
dṛṣṭaṃ tataḥ sarvamidaṃ bhavantaṃ manyāmahe tvāṃ praṇatāḥ sma nityam ।। 

nutiṃ mahārājakṛtāṃ ye paṭhiṣyanti mānavāḥ ।
cakravartipadaṃ prāpya te hi muktimavāpnuyuḥ ।। 

śrīcāturmahārājakṛtaṃ svayaṃbhūstavaṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no svayambhūstotram

jagatkṛte svayaṃbhuvamanādilīnamavyayam ।
tanorvipajjarātmakṛtsvayaṃbhuvaṃ namāmyaham ।। 

sahasrapatrapaṅkajaṃ lasatsukarṇikodbhavam ।
samastakāmanāpradaṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ namāmyaham ।। 

sahasrabhānurañjanaṃ niyutacandranandanam ।
surādilokavandanaṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ namāmyaham ।। 

tvameva rājase guṇairbhuvi sthito virājase ।
tridhātuka vibhāvase svayaṃbhuvaṃ namāmyaham ।। 

ayaṃ ka ityayaṃ hṛdā mīmāṃsituṃ na śaktavān ।
praghāsamātramīkṣitaḥ svayaṃbhuvaṃ namāmyaham ।। 

paṭhanti ye narā mudā svayaṃbhuvaḥ stutiṃ sadā ।
trivargasiddhimāpya te labhanti muktimeva tām ।। 

śrībṛhatsvayaṃbhūpurāṇoddhṛtaṃ śikhinirmitaṃ svayambhūstotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no vāgīśvaravarṇanāstotram

brahmādidevamanujāsurapūjitāṅgaṃ jñānādisarvanilayaṃ guṇarājavantam ।
jñānādhipaṃ guṇamayaṃ guṇavṛddhimantaṃ vāgīśvaraṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

vedādiśāstraracanākhilamantravijñaṃ stotraiḥ kathādibhiraśeṣasugītaśabdam ।
yaṃ kīryayanti munayo naravāṇyabhijñaṃ vāgīśvaraṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

jñānapradhānakaśarīramacintyabuddhiṃ vācaspatiṃ divi bhuvi stutakīrtidaṃ tam ।
jñāneśvaraṃ tribhuvaneśacarācaraṃ taṃ vāgīśvaraṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

ratnādiśilpaparikalpanapūrṇajñeyaṃ citraṃ vicitritaguṇaṃ janamānanīyam ।
sarvajñakārakadharād hṛdi brahmapuñjaṃ vāgīśvaraṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

caryāvidhau ratipatiṃ sthiradhairyabodhiṃ dhyānādhipaṃ vividhinā sukharañjanīyam ।
vidyāpratiṣṭhitaguruṃ bhuvanetipūrṇaṃ vāgīśvaraṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

vāṇīpatiṃ bhujacatuṣṭayabāṇacāpaṃ pustaṃ kṛpāṇamaniśaṃ kramaśo dadhānam ।
sarveṣṭadaṃ jagati yaccaṇāravindaṃ vāgīśvaraṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ namāmi ।। 

śrīvāgīśvaravarṇanāstotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no vāgvāṇīstotram

sarasvatīṃ namasyāmi cetanāṃ hṛdi saṃsthitām ।
kaṇṭhasthāṃ padmayoniṃ ca hrīṃkārasupriyāṃ sadā ।। 

matidāṃ varadāṃ caiva sarvakāmapradāyinīm ।
keśavasya priyāṃ devīṃ vīṇāhastāṃ varapradām ।। 

aiṃ hrīṃ mantrapriyāṃ caiva kumatidhvaṃsakāriṇīm ।
svaprakāśāṃ nirālambāmajñānatimirāpahām ।। 

mokṣapradāṃ sunityāṃ suvaradāṃ śodhanapriyām ।
ādityamaṇḍale līnāṃ praṇamāmi jinapriyām ।। 

jñānākārāṃ jagaddīpāṃ bhaktapāśavināśinīm ।
iti samyak stutā devī vāgīśena mahātmanā ।। 

ātmānaṃ darśayāmāsa śaradindusamaprabhā ।
sarasvatyuvāca varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadanta yatte manasi vartate ।। 

bṛhaspatiruvāca prasannā yadi me devī divyaṃ jñānaṃ pradīyatām ।
sarasvatyuvāca stotreṇānena ye bhaktyā māṃ stuvanti sadā narāḥ ।। 

labhante paramaṃ jñānaṃ mama tulyaparākramam ।
kavitvaṃ matprasādena tathā ca vipulaṃ yaśaḥ ।। 

trisandhyaṃ prayato bhūtvā yaḥ stotraṃ paṭhate naraḥ ।
tasya kaṇṭhe sadā vāsaṃ kariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

om aiṃ vāgvādini mama jihvāyāṃ eeṃ hrīṃ mantrasarasvati svāhā । bṛhaspatikṛtaṃ śrīvāgvāṇīstotraṃ samāptam ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no vajradevīstotram ācāryanāgārjunaviracitam

om namaḥ śrīyoginīdevyai

ḍākī yā sarvabuddhā sakalabhayaharā vyāpinī viśvamātā ekāsyā raktavarṇā trinayanamuditā khecarī śreṣṭhaśobhā ।
prajvālī divyadehā gagaṇakṛtapadā dvibhujā muktakeśā khaṭvāṅgaṃ vāmapāṇau dahinakaratikādhāriṇī svargarupā ।। 

nagnāṅgā grīvamālyā naraśirasahitā bhūṣaṇaṃ pañcamudr sattvānāṃ mārgamokṣā anuttaravaradā jñānasiddhipradātā ।
śrīdevī prāṇirakṣākṛtajagatahitā yoginī vajradīptistvatpādau padmarūpau praṇamitaśirasā naumi vidyādharīśe ।। 

bhagavatī mahādevī bhavatyāḥ śaraṇaṃ vajre ।
vande pādāmbuje nityaṃ bhajāmi tvāṃ prasīda me ।। 

jananī sarvabuddhānāṃ tvameva bodhidāyinī ।
sarveṣāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mātā hitānupālinī ।। 

sarvahitārthasaṃbhartrī sarvapāpaviśodhinī ।
duṣṭamāragaṇān kṣobhya mahānandasukhapradā ।। 

saddharmasādhanotsāhe balavīryaguṇapradā ।
niḥkleśastimitadhyānasamādhisukhadāyinī ।। 

prajñāguṇamahāratnaśrīsamṛddhipradāyinī ।
bhagavatyāḥ padāmbhoje śaraṇastho bhajāmyaham ।। 

namāmi vajravārāhīṃ sarvapāpapramocanīm ।
māravidhvaṃsinīṃ devīṃ buddhatvaphaladāyinīm ।। 

naumi śrīvajravārāhīṃ mantramūrtiṃ jineśvarīm ।
atyantavaradāṃ devīṃ ṛddhisiddhivarapradām ।। 

vairocanakulodbhūtāṃ muktakeśīṃ trilocanām ।
sandhyāsindūravarṇābhāṃ vande tvāṃ kuliśeśvarīm ।।

kare vajrakaroṭasthāṃ vande vajravilāsinīm ।।

samudbhūtāṃ sadā devīṃ vande tāṃ jñānaḍākinīm ।।

hāṃ hāṃ hāṃkāranādaiḥ kilikilitaravaiḥ bhūtavetālavṛndair hu huṃkāraiḥ samantānnarapiśitamukhai raktamālākulāṅgaiḥ ।
khaṭvāṅgaskannapāṇirnarakarakadharaḥ kāmarūpī virūpī piṅgākṣaḥ piṅgakeśaḥ śavagaṇanalakaḥ kṣetrapālo avatādvaḥ ।। 

pheṃ pheṃ pheṃkāranādaiḥ pratijanitabṛhadvahnigarbhāṅgavaktre mālāṃ kaṇṭhe nidhāya prakaṭabhayavapurbhūṣitāṅgopaśobhaḥ ।
īṣadraktādharoṣṭho asṛkasakalavṛtāmālinā muktapāṇiḥ klīṃ ḍāṃ klīṃ ḍāṃ ninādairvaradahanabhuvi kṣetrapaḥ pātu yuṣmān ।। 

kṣaṃ kṣaṃ kṣaṃ kṣāntimūrtiḥ kalakalakalakṛt kṣāntivṛddhiṃ prakurvan । krāntākrāntaikaviśvaḥ kahakahakathano nīlajīmūtavarṇaḥ ।
hrīṃ śrīṃ klīṃ mantradehaḥ paca paca dahanairjātamantraḥ samantād vighnānutsāryamāṇaḥ śamayatu niyataṃ śātravān kṣetrapālaḥ ।। 

hā hā hā hāṭṭahāsairatiśayabhayakṛt sarvadā asatpaśūnāṃ pāpānām, vighnahantā pratidivasamasau prāptasaṃbodhilābhaḥ ।
huṃ phaṭ huṃphaṭaninādaistribhuvanakuharaṃ pūrayan pūrṇaśaktiḥ pāyācchrīkṣetrapālaḥ kapilatarajaṭājūṭakleśāṅgabhāraḥ ।। 

khaṃ khaṃ khaṃ khaṅgapāṇirlalalalalalito rūpato raktapāṇiḥ raṃ raṃ raṃ raktanetro ru ru rudhirakaraścarcitaścaṇḍavegaḥ ।
kruṃ kruṃ kruṃ krodhadṛṣṭiḥ kuha kuha kuṭilaḥ kuñcitāśeṣaduṣṭaḥ ḍaṃ ḍaṃ ḍaṃ ḍāmarāṅgo ḍamarukasahito rakṣatāt kṣetrapālaḥ ।। 

yaṃ yaṃ yaṃ yāti viśvaṃ yamaniyamayuto yāmino ayāmino vā vaṃ vaṃ vaṃ vātavego jhaṭiti karakadhṛt prāptalokopacāraḥ ।
bhrūṃ bhrūṃ bhrūṃ bhīṣaṇāṅgo bhṛkuṭikṛtabhayo muktivān sādhakānāṃ kṣaṃ kṣaṃ kṣaṃ kṣemakārī kṣapayatu duritaṃ rakṣatāt kṣetrapālaḥ ।। 

klāṃ klāṃ klāṃ krāntimūrtistribhuvanamaniśaṃ kledayan sarvadā yaḥ paṃ paṃ paṃ pāśahastaḥ paraśudhṛtakaraḥ pālayan pālanīyān ।
mudrāṇāṃ mantramūrtistvamabhimataphalado mantriṇāṃ mantratulyaḥ kṣetrāṇāṃ pālako asau sakalajitatanuḥ pātu yuṣmāṃścirāyuḥ ।। 

klīṃ klīṃ klīṃ kṛttivāsā kṛtaripuniyamaḥ kleśitānāṃ sadeśaḥ kaṃ kaṃ kaṃ kapālamālī kalikaluṣaharaḥ kālavṛndābhakāyaḥ ।
caṃ caṃ caṃ caṇḍavegaḥ pracaritasamayāḥ kālabhūtaikalokaḥ saṃ saṃ saṃ saṃyatātmā samayaśubhaphalaṃ lakṣyatāṃ pātu yuṣmān ।। 

mantrāṇāṃ manrakāyo niyatayamadyutiḥ satpathe śūddhatīre ācāryaḥ sādhako vā japati ca niyataṃ puṇyavān jāyate asau ।
āyuḥ śrīḥ kīrtilakṣmīrdhṛtibalamatulaṃ śāntipuṣṭī prabhā ca sarvajñatvaṃ ca nityaṃ dinaniśamatulaṃ naśyate vighnajātam ।। 

śrīvajramahākālastotraṃ samāptam ।।

vajrasattva mahāsattva mahāyāna mahātmaka ।
mahāprabha mahāśuddha mahānātha namo astu te ।। 

vajrarāja mahāvajra vajra sarvatathāgata ।
mahāsattva mahāvīrya mahopāya namo astu te ।। 

vajrarāga mahāśuddha sarvasaukhya mahāsukha ।
sukhāgryānādinidhana mahākāma namo astu te ।। 

vajrasādhu mahātuṣṭi sādhukāra praharṣaka ।
mahāharṣa mahāmoda suprāmodya namo astu te ।। 

vajraratna mahārāja svābhiṣeka mahāmate ।
sarvaratna mahāśobhavibhūṣaṇa namo astu te ।। 

vajrateja mahāteja vajraprabha mahādyute ।
jinaprabha mahājvāla buddhaprabha namo astu te ।। 

vajraketu mahāketu mahādhvaja dhanaprada ।
ākāśaketo mahāyaṣṭi tyāgadhvaja namo astu te ।। 

vajrahāsa mahāhāsa mahāprītipramodana ।
prītivega ratiprīte dharmaprīte namo astu te ।। 

vajradharma mahādharma sarvadharmasuśodhaka ।
buddhadharma sudharmāgrya rāgadharma namo astu te ।। 

vajratīkṣṇa mahākośa prajñājñāna mahāmate ।
pāpacchedamahākhaḍga buddhaśastra namo astu te ।। 

vajrahetu mahācakra buddhacakra mahānidhe ।
sarvamaṇḍaladharmāgra dharmacakra namo astu te ।। 

vajrabhāṣa mahābhāṣa niṣprapañca mahākṣara ।
anakṣara mahājāpa buddhavāca namo astu te ।। 

vajrakarma sukarmāgrya mahākarma sukarmakṛt ।
guhyapūja mahāpūja buddhapūja namo astu te ।। 

vajrarakṣa mahāvarma kavacāgrya mahādṛḍha ।
mahārakṣa mahāsāra buddhavīrya namo astu te ।। 

vajrayakṣa mahākrodha sarvaduṣṭabhayānaka ।
sarvabuddhamahopāya agrayakṣa namo astu te ।। 

mahāsandhi mahāmudra mahāsamayabandhaka ।
mahāmuṣṭe samudrāgrya vajramuṣṭe namo astu te ।। 

vandyo mānyaśca pūjyaśca satkartavyastathāgataiḥ ।
yasmādanādinidhanaṃ bodhicittaṃ tvamucyase ।। 

tvāmāsādya jināḥ sarve bodhisattvāśca śauriṇaḥ ।
saṃbhūtāḥ saṃbhaviṣyanti buddhabodhyagrahetavaḥ ।। 

namaste vajrasattvāya vajraratnāya te namaḥ ।
namaste vajradharmāya namaste vajrakarmaṇe ।। 

tvāmabhiṣṭutya nāmāgraiḥ praṇamya ca subhāvataḥ ।
yatpuṇyaṃ tena sarvo hi buddhabodhimavāpnuyāt ।। 

idamuccārayetsamyag nāmāṣṭaśatamuttamam ।

śrīvajrapāṇināmāṣṭottaraśatastotraṃ samāptam ।।
