vande śrī

vajrasattvaṃ bhuvanavaraguruṃ sarvabuddhaṃ bhavantaṃ nānārūpaṃ jinendraṃ timirabhayaharaṃ nirmitaṃ meruśāntam ।
dharmādhāraṃ munīnāṃ jinaguṇaśubhadaṃ maṇḍalaṃ vajradhātuṃ sarvānandaikarūpaṃ paramasukhamayaṃ dehināṃ mokṣahetum ।। 

ajñānagāḍhatimirārṇavamagnasattvamohāndhakāratamavāraṇacandraraśmiḥ ।
jñānaṃ prakāśya paripūritavīryadhyānaṃ śrīvajrasattvamasamaṃ śirasā namāmi ।। 

yasmin surāsurasurendranarendravṛndāstvatpādapadmapatitā bhramarāḥ śirobhiḥ ।
tatsiddhisādhanapayodhimahānidhānaṃ śrīlokanāthacaraṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ prayāmi ।। 

buddhaṃ trailokyanāthaṃ suravaranamitaṃ pārasaṃsāratīrṇaṃ dhīraṃ gāmbhīryavantaṃ sakalaguṇanidhiṃ dharmarājābhiṣiktam ।
tṛṣṇāmohāndhakāraṃ kalikaluṣaharaṃ kāmalobhādavantaṃ taṃ vande śākyasiṃhaṃ praṇamitaśirasā sarvakālaṃ namāmi ।। 

hrīṃkārasaṃbhavaṃ nāthaṃ karuṇāsnigdhamānasam ।
amoghapāśanāmānaṃ lokanāthaṃ namāmyaham ।। 

māmakī locanā tārā padminī jinadhātave ।
sarvabuddhālayaṃ caityaṃ dharmadhātuṃ namāmi tam ।। 

namastāre ture vīre tuttāre bhayanāśini ।
ture sarvāture kāle svāhākāraṃ namāmyaham ।। 

saddharmapuṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sarvajñaguṇasāgaram ।
samantabhadraśāstāraṃ śākyasiṃhaṃ namāmyaham ।। 

śrīvajrasattvastotraṃ samāptam ।।

om namaḥ śrīvajrayoginyai

devāsuranaravanditacaraṇe bhavamagnoddharaṇārpitacaraṇe ।
tvayi rodimi nutisavyapadeśaḥ kiṃ paśyasi punaraniśamaśeṣam ।। 

mātardevi kirasi kaṇamuṣṭiṃ janayad yajñasutaḥ kimatuṣṭim ।
vajravārāhi narāhisurāṇāṃ tvaṃ śaraṇaṃ tava nāmaparāṇām ।। 

harikara śikhiphaṇitaskarabhītistvatparacitte naiva sameti ।
mātardevi nibhālaya mahyaṃ kiṃ sahase mama duḥkhamasahyam ।। 

tarjanavajrakaroṭa dhāriṇi duṣṭaṃ tuṣṭaya māranivāriṇi ।
abhinavakomalakaracaraṇāṅgi trivalisamucchadasaptavibhaṅgi ।। 

grāhyagrāhakabhāvaviśuddhe pādakarāṅgulijālapinaddhe ।
āyatapārśvāṅgulikaracaraṇe dhvastavyādhijarājanimaraṇe ।। 

udgatareṇurūrdhvagataromā vajrayogavivṛtāmṛtadhāmā ।

subhru tanūdari madhyakṛśāṅgi karṇāntāyatalocanabhṛṅgi ।
ḍākinye viśvamaśeṣaṃ loko vetti na te bahuveṣam ।। 

yatnamṛte jagadarthasamṛddhiścintitamātrajanepsitasiddhiḥ ।
mūḍho vetti na duṣkṛtakarma prāvṛṣīva na śilāṅkurajanma ।। 

andha ivārkaśaśāṅkādarśī pāpajano hyanubhāvasparśī ।
cintāmaṇimajñā na vidanti prajñe tvasya phalāni phalanti ।। 

cakrāṅkitakarapādamanojñe jñānānalabhasmīkṛtasaṅge ।
kāyavacanamanasā kṛtaduritaṃ rāgadveṣamohaparikari tam ।। 

taddiśāmi tava devi samakṣaṃ yāvadyāmi na durgatipakṣam ।
manaḥ paramārthaṃ tanustava vedī sa bhavati naiva duritaparikhedī ।। 

lakṣaṇanikhilālakṣitagātre sakalānuvyañjanagatapātre ।
navayauvanamadamantharapiṇḍe calakuṇḍalayugamaṇḍitagaṇḍe ।। 

tuṅganitambaghanastanabhāre galakālambiniraṃśuka hāre ।
saṃvaramadhupavicumbimukhābje tadbhujayugaparirabdhahṛdabje ।। 

nirbharasuratasukhāvikalākṣi muktaśiroruhavasananirapekṣe ।
herukarāhudaṣṭamukhacandre sasmitaracita hūṃ hūṃ kṛtamantre ।। 

patimaulisthitavidhumamṛṣantī kimu candrārkau vapu muṣantī ।
mātaste jagadanupamarūpaṃ tadvicāraya paramārtha sa rūpam ।। 

kleśadāhiṃ śamanāmṛtavacanaṃ tadvineyajanaśuddhiviracanam ।
padminīti nalināmalagandhaḥ karuṇāparajagadarthanibandhaḥ ।। 

divyasudhādhara rasapānaṃ tajjagadadvayabodhinidhānam ।
pratyaṅgasparśo apyanimittaṃ sahajāmbudhiviplāvitacittam ।। 

kiṃ tvaṃ mātaḥ kariṣyasi tābhiḥ ṣaṭtriṃśacchatakoṭyabalābhiḥ ।
yadyanyāṃ manute bahutātastadvihāya jhagiti dehi nu mātaḥ ।। 

nāḍīcakranirodha […] mahāsukhasaṃvara ।
devi tvaṃ śatabhāvavikalpā śūnyasamādhirapākṛtatulyā ।। 

śūnyakṛpe sahajādvayamuktaṃ vajrāya namidamavadhi bhaktam ।
bhāvābhāvasamastākāśavyāpī bhavati sa tattvavikāśaḥ ।। 

udbhavanti tata eva vimokṣā bodhipakṣanikhilapratipakṣāḥ ।
buddhānāmāveṇikadharmaḥ sattvarāśiparipācitakarmaḥ ।। 

yadvā yānatrayaniryāṇaṃ dhūmādikamapi cāparimāṇam ।
tvadbhaktyā yadalambhi śubhaṃ me bhavatu mano bhavatīparamaṃ me ।
sakalakaluṣarahitaṃ guṇasindhustvatparamaṃ hyata eva na bandhuḥ ।। 

guhyasamayasādhanatantre śrīvajravilāsinīstotraṃ samāptam । kṛtiriyaṃ mahāpaṇḍitavibhūticandrapādānām ।।

sarvākāravaropete namaste vajrayogini ।।

sadasatkalpanātīte namaste vajrayogini ।। 

śyāmapītādinirmukte varṇāvarṇavivarjite ।
prajñāpāramitāmātarnamaste vajrayogini ।। 

nirvikalpe nirālambe niṣprapañce nirālaye ।
viyadvayāpi nairātmye namaste vajrayogini ।। 

sarvaratnavidāṃ pātre janani vajrayogini ।
namaste vajravārāhi namaste vajrayogini ।। 

tvaṃ sadgurumukhakamalānnirgatā kāmarūpiṇī ।
mahā ajñānavināśāya namaste vajrayogini ।। 

iti guṇayuktāyā māturvidhāyaikaviṃśikām ।
puṇyaṃ yadavāptaṃ tena janāḥ santu pūrṇatvam ।। 

śrīvajrayoginīpraṇāmaikaviṃśikā samāptā ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no vajrayoginyāḥ piṇḍārthastutiḥ siddhācāryavirūpādaviaracitā

om namo vajrayoginyai । om namo buddhadharmasaṃghebhyaḥ । om namo gurubuddhabodhisattvebhyaḥ । om namo locanādidaśavajravilāsinībhyaḥ । namo yamāntakādidaśakroḍha vīrebhyaḥ । vārāhī śauṇḍinī caiva caṇḍālī ḍombinī tathā ।

naṭanī rajakī brāhmī kapālinī ca sāsa tā ।। 

amṛtā amṛtakuṇḍalī ca jñānajyotiḥprakāśikā ।
sarvāśāvīradevīnāmiyamekā mahāsukhā ।। 

śūnyatā gīyate cāsau parāśaktiḥ parātparā ।
amṛtordhvamanā divyā upāyā nityavāhinī ।। 

khecarī bhūcarī caiva pātālavāsinī tathā ।
pravi ṣṭhāpūraṇī nityaṃ trailokyakṣobhatī tathā ।। 

bindunādakalā devī candrasūryātmikā hi sā ।
nairmāṇikī caiva saṃbhāgī ca mahāsukhā ।। 

bindunādakalātītā prajñāpāramitā matā ।
sarvabhāvasvabhāvā hi sarvabhāvavivarjitā ।। 

pralayotpattihīnā ca pralayotpattikāriṇī ।
śāśvatatvāt sthitā proktā śāśvatena ca varjitā ।। 

gambhīrāliṅgitodārā mahārthā svadhimuktikā ।
śūnyatātrayahīnā ca prabhāsvarasvarūpiṇī ।। 

ekārākṣararūpā ca vaṃkārākṣarasaṃgatā ।
vicitrādikṣaṇairyuktā caturānandarūpiṇī ।। 

bāhyamaṇḍalacakre api sphurantī ca trikāyataḥ ।
kāyavākacittabhāveṣu kāyavākacittabhūṣaṇī ।। 

atītya kāyavākacittaiḥ samatvena ca madhyagā ।
nairātmyarūpiṇī devī tathatāyāṃ pratiṣṭhitā ।। 

kamalakuliśākrāntaśūnyatātrayarūpiṇī ।
lalanārasanāyogādavadhūtī mahāsukhā ।। 

saṃsāratāraṇī caiṣāṃ tathā tāsāṃ pratītyajā ।
yāṃ labdhvā yoginīṃ muktā bhavasaṃsārabandhanāt ।। 

ityeṣā ṛddhidā proktā siddhidā caiva yoginī ।
mokṣadvāraparā caiva satatābhyāsakāriṇām ।। 

vajravat kurute dehaṃ rasasiddhiṃ dadāti ca ।
gurupādaprasādena labdheyaṃ vajrayoginī ।। 

ya tasyāḥ pāṭhamātreṇa puṇyasaṃbhāramādarāt ।
prāpnoti satataṃ yogī jñānasaṃbhārasaṃbhṛtaḥ ।। 

śrīguhyasamayatantre piṇḍārthāḥ ṣoḍaśaślokāstrikāyavajrayoginyāḥ samāptāḥ । kṛtiriyaṃ siddhācāryaśrīvirupādānāmiti ।।

digital sanskrit buddhist canon, stotra section, text no vajrayoginyāḥ stutipraṇidhānam siddhācāryavirūpādaviracitam

om namaḥ śrī vajrayoginyai, namobuddhadharmasaṃghebhyaḥ, namo gurubuddhabodhisattvebhyaḥ, namo locanādidaśavajravilāsinībhyaḥ, namo yamāntakādidaśakrodhavīrebhyaḥ saprajñebhyaḥ ।
om o ā hūṃ iti kāyavākacita indriyavijñānāni, vākacittāni manovijñānāni, paracittajñānābhijñā, parakāyapraveśābhijñā puṇḍarīkeṣu nābhisthe raktasūrya maṇḍalaḥ ।। 

dharmodayā padmamadhye sindūrāruṇarūpiṇī ।
triśṛṅgā hi trikoṇā vā catuḥpīṭhasamanvitā ।। 

hrīṃkāraṃ madhyabhāge asyāḥ pītavarṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।
tadbhavā pītavarṇā ca avadhūtyā svayaṃ sthitā ।। 

lalanāyāṃ tu suśyāmā rasanāyāṃ ca gaurikā ।
pratyālīḍhapadā nāmnā madhye pītā manoramā ।। 

trimārge saṃsthitā devī trikāyavajrayoginī ।
seyaṃ nāmnā bhavedekā sarvasambuddhaḍākinī ।। 

trailokye divyarūpā ca sarvāśāparipūrikā ।
svakartinā kartitaṃ ca vāmahaste svamastakam ।। 

dakṣiṇe asyā sthitā kartirjagato duḥkhacchedinī ।
asyā vāme sthitā śyāmā nāmnā sā varavarṇinī ।। 

karparaḥ savyahaste ca kartirvāme ca saṃsthitā ।
dakṣiṇe caiva pītā vai vajravairocanī sthitā ।। 

kartikā dakṣiṇe haste vāme kapāladhāriṇī ।
pratyālīḍhapadā devī nagnikā tu viśeṣataḥ ।। 

karau ca dvau tayoḥ pādau viparītau tathā sthitau ।
buddhānāṃ jananī madhyā samyaksambuddharūpiṇī ।। 

akṣayā subhagā nityaṃ hantrī ca mṛtyujanmanoḥ ।
dharmasaṃbhoganirmāṇamahāsukhasvarūpiṇī ।। 

seyaṃ tribhuvane devī rājaye candravatsadā ।
kabandhādavadhūtyāśca praviśetsvamukheṣvasṛk ।। 

lalanārasanābhyāṃ ca niḥsṛtya śirasi tathā ।
karūṇāraktarūpeṇa pibantī sarvaśāntaye ।। 

duḥkhaṃ saṃprekṣya lokānāṃ caturmāraniṣūdinī ।
daurmanasyādi kartyā ca kartantī sarvameva tat ।। 

stutā hi jinamātastvaṃ suprasīda bhavārṇave ।
svārthaṃ kartuṃ parārthaṃ ca bhavāmyahaṃ yathā kṣamaḥ ।। 

tattvayā devī kartavyamanugrahaṃ mayi sṛja ।
bālo ahamajñarūpī ca kāyavākacittadoṣataḥ ।। 

gurubhaktiṃ na jāne ahaṃ tvadbhaktiṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
ityākalaya lokeśi kṛpā mayi vidhīyatām ।। 

kāyavākacetasāṃ sāmyaṃ kuru me tvaṃ prasādataḥ ।
yena muñcāmi saṃsāraṃ ṣaḍgatiṃ na viśāmyaham ।। 

yathā ca vajravaddeho yāvanmukto bhavāmyaham ।
māraiḥ sarvaiḥ parityakto yathā kāyo bhavenmama ।। 

līlayā siddhibhāgāḥ syurnirvighnaḥ sarvasiddhibhāk ।
sarvasādhanasiddhi syāt kāyaścaivājarāmaraḥ ।। 

trāsanaṃ sarvamārāṇāṃ sarvāśāparipūraṇam ।
dehi me tvaṃ varāṃ siddhiṃ hitvā caiva gamāgamam ।। 

mano vilīyatāṃ devi pañcendriyānusaṃyutam ।
siddhyecca vajrasattvāyuryauvanārogyasatsukham ।। 

tvatprasādānmahāmudrā sarveṣāmeva saṃbhavet ।
devāsuramanuṣyāśca yatra yatra ca saṃsthitāḥ ।
sukhinaste ca sarve syurbuddhatvaphalalābhinaḥ ।। 

śrīguhyasamayatantre trikāyavajrayoginyāḥ stutipraṇidhānaṃ samāptam । kṛtiriyaṃ siddhācārya śrīvirūpādānām ।।

nāḍikāsamayavajrapadmagaṃ tvāṃ namāmyubhayacittaherukam ।। 

guhyakokanadakarṇikāntaravyomapañcakamahānabhaḥsthitam ।

bhagavatyai āryaśrīvasudhārāyai divyarūpī surūpī ca saumyarūpī balapradā ।
vasudharī vasudhāraṇī vasuśrī śrīkarī varā ।। 

dharaṇī dhāraṇī dhātā śaraṇyā bhaktavatsalā ।
prajñāpāramitā devī prajñā śrībuddhivardhinī ।। 

vidyādharī śivā sūkṣmā śāstā sarvatra mātṛkā ।
taruṇī tāru ṇī devī vidyādāneśvareśvarī ।। 

bhūṣitā bhūtamātā ca sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā ।
durdāntatrāsanī bhītā ugrā ugraparākramā ।। 

dānapāramitā devī varṣaṇī divyarūpiṇī ।
nidhānaṃ sarvamāṅgalyā kīrtirlakṣmīryaśaḥśubhā ।। 

dahanī mālinī caṇḍī śabarī sarvamātrikā ।
kṛtāntaśāsanī raudrī kaumārī viśvarūpiṇī ।। 

vīryapāramitā devī jagadānandarocanī ।
tāpasī ugrarūpī ca ṛddhisiddhibalapradā ।। 

dhanyā puṇyā mahābhāgā ajitā jitavikramā ।
jagadekahitā vidyā saṃgrāme tāraṇī śubhā ।। 

kṣāntipāramitā devī śīlinī dhyānadhyāyino ।
padminī padmadhārī ca padmapriyā padmāsanī ।। 

śuddharūpī mahātejā hemavarṇā prabhākarī ।
cintāmaṇimahādevī prajñāpustakadhāriṇī ।।

traidhātukaṃ mahā ādi divyābharaṇabhūṣiṇī ।। 

mātarī sarvabuddhānāṃ ratnadhāte śvareśvarī ।
śūnyatā bhāvanī devī bhāvābhāvavivarjitā ।। 

vainye ya kiṃ na vinyastā divyakleśanichedanī ।
bhī dinī sarvamārāṇāṃ saptapātālakṣobhinī ।। 

brahmāṇī vedamātā ca guhyā ca guhyavāsinī ।
sarasvatī viśālākṣī caturbrahmavihāriṇī ।। 

tāthāgatī mahāramyā vajriṇī dharmadhāriṇī ।
karmadhāteśvarī vidyā viśvajvālābhamaṇḍalī ।। 

bodha nī sarvasattvānāṃ bodhyaṅgakṛtaśekharī ।
dhyānā dhīrmuktisaṃpannā advayadvayabhāvinī ।। 

sarvārthasādhanī bhadrā strīrūpāmitavikramā ।

vāgīśvarī mahāśāntirgoptrī dhātrī dhanapradā ।
strīrūpadhāriṇī siddhā yoginī yogajeśvarī ।।

sārthavāhakṛpādṛṣṭiḥ sarvatāthāgatātmakī ।।

atha vajradharaḥ śrīmān durdāntadamakaḥ paraḥ ।

vibuddhapuṇḍarīkākṣaḥ protphullakamalānanaḥ ।
prollālayan vajravaraṃ svakareṇa muhurmuhaḥ ।। 

bhṛkuṭītaraṅgapramukhairanantairvajrapāṇibhiḥ ।
durdāntadamakairvīrairvīravībhatsarupibhiḥ ।। 

ullālayadibhiḥ svakaraiḥ prasphuradvajrakoṭibhiḥ ।
prajñopāyamahākaruṇājagadarthakaraiḥ paraiḥ ।। 

hṛṣṭatuṣṭāśayairmuditaiḥ krodhavigraharupibhiḥ ।

praṇamya nāthaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ tathāgatam ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā idamāha sthito agrataḥ ।। 

maddhitāya mamārthāya anukampāya me vibho ।

hitāya sarvasattvānāmanuttaraphalāptaye ।।

bhagavan! jñānakāyasya mahoṣṇīṣasya gīṣpateḥ ।

yastvaṃ jagaddhitārthāya mahākaruṇayānvitaḥ ।।

śṛṇu tvamekāgramanāstatsādhu bhagavanniti ।। 

iti prativacanajñānagāthāḥ ṣaṭ ।

mantravidyādharakulaṃ vyavalokya kulatrayam ।। 

lokalokottarakulaṃ lokālokakulaṃ mahat ।

jñānamūrtirahaṃ buddho buddhānāṃ tryadhvavartinām ।। 

om vajratīkṣṇaduḥkhacchedaprajñājñānamūrtaye ।
jñānakāyavāgīśvarārapacanāya te namaḥ ।। 

iti māyājālābhisaṃbodhikramagāthāstisraḥ ।

tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ saṃbuddho akārasambhavaḥ ।
akāraḥ sarvavarṇāgryo mahārthaḥ paramākṣaraḥ ।। 

mahāprāṇo hyanutpādo vāgadāhāravarjitaḥ ।
sarvābhilāpahetvgryaḥ sarvavāksuprabhāsvaraḥ ।। 

mahāmahamahārāgaḥ sarvasattvaratiṅkaraḥ ।
mahāmahamahādveṣaḥ sarvakleśamahāripuḥ ।। 

mahāmahamahāmoho mūḍhadhīmohasūdanaḥ ।
mahāmahamahākrodho mahākrodharipurmahān ।। 

mahāmahamahālobhaḥ sarvalobhaniṣūdanaḥ ।
mahākāmo mahāsaukhyo mahāmodo mahāratiḥ ।। 

mahārupo mahākāyo mahāvarṇo mahāvapuḥ ।
mahānāmā mahodāro mahāvipulamaṇḍalaḥ ।। 

mahāprajñāyudhadharo mahākleśāṅkuśo agraṇīḥ ।
mahāyaśā mahākīrtirmahājyotirmahādyutiḥ ।। 

mahāmāyādharo vidvān mahāmāyārthasādhakaḥ ।
mahāmāyāratirato mahāmāyendrajālikaḥ ।। 

mahādānapatiḥ śreṣṭho mahāśīladharo agraṇīḥ ।
mahākṣāntidharo dhīro mahāvīryaparākramaḥ ।। 

mahādhyānasamādhistho mahāprajñāśarīradhṛk ।
mahābalo mahāpāyaḥ praṇidhirjñānasāgaraḥ ।। 

mahāmaitrīmayo ameyo mahākāruṇiko agradhīḥ ।
mahāprajño mahādhīmān mahopāyo mahākṛtiḥ ।। 

mahāṛddhibalopeto mahāvego mahājavaḥ ।
maharddhiko maheśākhyo mahābalaparākramaḥ ।। 

mahābhavādrisaṃbhettā mahāvajradharo dhanaḥ ।
mahākrūro mahāraudro mahābhayabhayaṅkara ।। 

mahāvidyottamo nātho mahāmantrottamo guruḥ ।
mahāyānanayāruḍho mahāyānanayottamaḥ ।। 

iti vajradhātumaṇḍalajñānagāthāścaturdaśa ।

mahāvairocano buddho mahāmaunī mahāmuniḥ ।
mahāmantranayodbhūto mahāmantranayātmakaḥ ।। 

daśapāramitāprāpto daśapāramitāśrayaḥ ।
daśapāramitāśuddhirdaśapāramitānayaḥ ।। 

daśabhūmīśvaro nātho daśabhūmipratiṣṭhitaḥ ।
daśajñānaviśuddhātmā daśajñānaviśuddhadhṛk ।। 

daśākāro daśārthārtho munīndro daśabalo vibhuḥ ।
aśeṣaviśvārthakaro daśākāravaśī mahān ।। 

anādirniṣprapañcātmā śuddhātmā tathatātmakaḥ ।
bhūtavādī yathāvādī tathākārī ananyavāk ।। 

advayo dvayavādī ca bhūtakoṭivyavasthitaḥ ।
nairātmyasiṃhanirṇādī kutīthryamṛgabhīkaraḥ ।। 

sarvatrago amoghagatistathāgatamanojavaḥ ।
jino jitārirvijayo cakravartī mahābalaḥ ।। 

gaṇamukhyo gaṇācāryo gaṇeśo gaṇapatirvaśī ।
mahānubhāvo dhaureyo ananyaneyo mahānayaḥ ।। 

vāgiśo vākpatirvāgmī vācaspatiranantagoḥ ।
satyavāk satyavādī ca catuḥsatyopadeśakaḥ ।। 

avaivartiko hyanāgāmo khaḍgaḥ pratyekanāyakaḥ ।
nānāniryāṇaniryāto mahābhūtaikakāraṇaḥ ।। 

arhan kṣīṇāsravo bhikṣurvītarāgo jitendriyaḥ ।
kṣemaprāpto abhayaprāptaḥ śītībhūto hyānāvilaḥ ।। 

vidyācaraṇasaṃpannaḥ sugato lokavitparaḥ ।
nirmamo nirahaṅkāraḥ satyadvayanayasthitaḥ ।। 

saṃsārapārakoṭisthaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ sthalasthitaḥ ।
kaivalyajñānaniṣṭhiyutaḥ prajñāśastro vidāraṇaḥ ।। 

saddharmmo dharmarāḍ bhāsvān lokālokakaraḥ paraḥ ।
dharmeśvaro dharmarājaḥ śreyomārgopadeśakaḥ ।। 

siddhārthaḥ siddhasaṃkalpaḥ sarvasaṃkalpavarjitaḥ ।
nirvikalpo akṣayo dhāturdharmadhātuḥ paro avyayaḥ ।। 

puṇyavān puṇyasaṃbhāro jñānaṃ jñānākaraṃ mahat ।
jñānavān sadasajjñānī saṃbhāradvayasaṃbhṛtaḥ ।। 

śāśvato viśvarāḍ yogī dhyānaṃ dhyeyo dhiyāṃpatiḥ ।
pratyātmavedyo hyacalaḥ paramādyastrikāyadhṛk ।। 

pañcakāyātmako buddhaḥ pañcajñānātmako vibhuḥ ।
pañcabuddhātmamukuṭaḥ pañcacakṣurasaṅgadhṛk ।। 

janakaḥ sarvabuddhānāṃ buddhaputraḥ parovaraḥ ।
prajñābhavodbhavo yonirdharmayonirbhavāntakṛt ।। 

ghanaikasāro vajrātmā sadyojāto jagatpatiḥ ।
gaganodbhavaḥ svayambhūḥ prajñājñānānalo mahān ।। 

vairocano mahādīptirjñānajyotirvirocanaḥ ।
jagatpradīpo jñānolko mahātejāḥ prabhāsvaraḥ ।। 

vidyārājo agramantreśo mantrarājo mahārthakṛt ।
mahoṣṇīṣo adbhutoṣṇīṣo viśvadarśī viyatpatiḥ ।। 

sarvabuddhātmabhāvāgryo jagadānandalocanaḥ ।
viśvarupī vidhātā ca pūjyo, mānyo mahāṛṣiḥ ।। 

kulatrayadharo mantrī mahāsamayamantradhṛk ।
ratnatrayadharaḥ śreṣṭhastriyānottamadeśakaḥ ।। 

amoghapāśo vijayī vajrapāśo mahāgrahaḥ ।
vajrāṅkuśo mahāpāśaḥ vajrabhairavabhīkaraḥ ।। 

iti suviśuddhadharmadhātujñānagāthāḥ pādonapañcaviṃśatiḥ ।

krodharāṭ ṣaṇmukho bhīmaḥ ṣaṇṇetraḥ ṣaḍbhujo balī ।
daṃṣṭrākarālaḥ kaṅkālo halāhalaḥ śatānanaḥ ।। 

yamāntako vighnarājo vajravego bhayaṅkaraḥ ।
vighuṣṭavajro hṛdvajro māyāvajro mahodaraḥ ।। 

kuliśeśo vajrayonirvajramaṇḍo nabhopamaḥ ।
acalaikajaṭāṭopo gajacarmapaṭārdradhṛk ।। 

hāhākāro mahāghoro hīhīkāro bhayānakaḥ ।
aṭṭahāso mahāhāso vajrahāso mahāravaḥ ।। 

vajrasattvo mahāsattvo vajrarājo mahāsukhaḥ ।
vajracaṇḍo mahāmodo vajrahūṃkārahūṃkṛtiḥ ।। 

vajrabāṇāyudhadharo vajrakhaḍgo nikṛntanaḥ ।
viśvavajradharo bajrī ekavajrī raṇañjahaḥ ।। 

vajrajvālākarālākṣo vajrajvālāśiroruhaḥ ।
vajrāveśo mahāveśaḥ śatākṣo vajralocanaḥ ।। 

vajraromāṅkuratanurvajraromaikavigrahaḥ ।
vajrakoṭinakhārambho vajrasāraghanacchavi ।। 

vajramālādharaḥ śrīmān vajrābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।
hāhāṭṭahāso nirghoṣo vajraghoṣaḥ ṣaḍakṣaraḥ ।। 

mañjughoṣo mahānādastrailokyaikaravo mahān ।
ākāśadhātuparyantaghoṣo ghoṣavatāṃ varaḥ ।। 

ityādarśajñānagāthāḥ pādena sārdhaṃ daśa ।

tathatābhūtanairātmyabhūtakoṭiranakṣaraḥ ।
śūnyatāvādivṛṣabho gambhīrodāragarjanaḥ ।। 

dharmaśaṅkho mahāśabdo dharmagaṇḍī mahāraṇaḥ ।
apratiṣṭhitanirvāṇo daśadigdharmadundubhiḥ ।। 

arupo rupavānagryo nānārupo manomayaḥ ।
sarvarupāvabhāsaśrīraśeṣapratibimbadhṛk ।। 

apradhṛṣyo maheśākhyastraidhātukamaheśvaraḥ ।
samucchritāryamārgastho dharmaketurmahodaya ।। 

trailokyaikakumārāṅgaḥ sthaviro vṛddhaḥ prajāpati ।
dvātriṃśallakṣaṇadharaḥ kāntastrailokyasundaraḥ ।। 

lokajñānaguṇācāryo lokācāryo viśāradaḥ ।
nāthastrātā trilokāptaḥ śaraṇaṃ tāyyanuttaraḥ ।। 

gaganābhogasambhogaḥ sarvajñajñānasāgaraḥ ।
avidyāṇḍakośasaṃbhettā bhavapañjaradāraṇaḥ ।। 

śamitāśeṣasaṃkleśaḥ saṃsārārṇavapāragaḥ ।
jñānābhiṣekamukuṭaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। 

triduḥkhaduḥkhaśamanastryanto anantastrimuktigaḥ ।
sarvāvaraṇanirmukta ākāśasamatāṃ gataḥ ।। 

sarvakleśamalātītastryadhvānadhvagatiṃ gataḥ ।
sarvasattvamahānāgo guṇaśekharaśekharaḥ ।। 

sarvopadhivinirmukto vyomavatrmani susthitaḥ ।
mahācintāmaṇidharaḥ sarvaratnottamo vibhuḥ ।। 

mahākalpataruḥ sphīto mahābhadraghaṭottamaḥ ।
sarvasattvārthakṛtkarttā hitaiṣī sattvavatsalaḥ ।। 

śubhāśubhajñaḥ kālajñaḥ samayajñaḥ samayo vibhuḥ ।
sattvendriyajño velajño vimuktitrayakovidaḥ ।। 

guṇī guṇajño dharmajñaḥ praśasto maṅgalodayaḥ ।
sarvamaṅgalamāṅgalyaḥ kīrtirlakṣmīryaśaḥ śubhaḥ ।। 

mahotsavo mahāśvāso mahānando mahāratiḥ ।
satkāraḥ satkṛtirbhūtiḥ pramodaḥ śrīryaśaspatiḥ ।। 

vareṇyo varadaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇottamaḥ ।
mahābhayāriḥ pravaro niḥśeṣabhayanāśanaḥ ।। 

śikhī śikhaṇḍī jaṭilo jaṭī mauṇḍī kirīṭimān ।
pañcānanaḥ pañcaśikhaḥ pañcacīrakaśekharaḥ ।। 

mahābratadharo mauñjī brahmacārī bratottamaḥ ।
mahātapāstaponiṣṭhaḥ snātako gautamo agraṇī ।। 

brahmavid brāhmaṇo brahmā brahmanirvāṇamāptavān ।
muktirmokṣo vimokṣāṅgo vimuktiḥ śāntatā śivaḥ ।। 

nirvāṇaṃ nirvṛtiḥ śāntiḥ śreyo niryāṇamantagaḥ ।
sukhaduḥkhāntakṛnniṣṭhā vairāgyamupadhikṣayaḥ ।। 

ajayo anupamo avyakto nirābhāso nirañjanaḥ ।
niṣkalaḥ sarvago vyāpī sūkṣmo bījamanāśravaḥ ।। 

arajo virajo vimalo vāntadoṣo nirāmayaḥ ।
suprabuddho vibuddhātmā sarvajñaḥ sarvavitparaḥ ।। 

vijñānadharmatātīto jñānamadvayarupadhṛk ।
nirvikalpo nirābhogastryadhvasaṃbuddhakāryakṛt ।। 

anādinidhano buddha ādibuddho niranvayaḥ ।
jñānaikacakṣuramalo jñānamūrtistathāgataḥ ।। 

vāgīśvaro mahāvādī vādirāḍ vādipuṅgavaḥ ।
vadatāṃvaro variṣṭho vādisiṃho aparājitaḥ ।। 

samantadarśī prāmodyastejomālī sudarśanaḥ ।
śrīvatsaḥ suprabho dīptirbhābhāsurakaradyutiḥ ।। 

mahābhiṣagvaraḥ śreṣṭhaḥ śalyahartā niruttaraḥ ।
aśeṣabhaiṣajyataruḥ kleśavyādhirmahāripuḥ ।। 

trailokyatilakaḥ kāntaḥ śrīmān nakṣatramaṇḍalaḥ ।
daśadigvyomaparyyanto dharmadhvajamahocchrayaḥ ।। 

jagacchatraikavipulo maitrīkaruṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।
padmanṛtyeśvaraḥ śrīmān ratnacchatro mahāvibhuḥ ।। 

sarvabuddhamahārājaḥ sarvabuddhātmabhāvadhṛk ।
sarvabuddhamahāyogaḥ sarvabuddhaikaśāsanaḥ ।। 

vajraratnābhiṣekaśrīḥ sarvaratnādhipeśvaraḥ ।
sarvalokeśvarapatiḥ sarvavajradharādhipaḥ ।। 

sarvabuddhamahācittaḥ sarvabuddhamanogatiḥ ।
sarvabuddhamahākāyaḥ sarvabuddhasarasvatī ।। 

vajrasūryyamahāloko vajrenduvimalaprabhaḥ ।
virāgādimahārāgo viśvavarṇojjvalaprabhaḥ ।। 

sambuddhavajraparyaṅko buddhasaṅgītidharmadhṛk ।
buddhapadmodbhavaḥ śrīmān sarvajñajñānakoṣadhṛk ।। 

viśvamāyādharo rājā buddhavidyādharo mahān ।
vajratīkṣṇo mahākhaḍgo viśuddhaḥ paramākṣaraḥ ।। 

duḥkhacchedamahāyānavajradharmamahāyudhaḥ ।
jinajig vajragāmbhīryo vajrabuddhiryathārthavit ।। 

sarvapāramitāpūrī sarvabhūmivibhūṣaṇaḥ ।
viśuddhadharmanairātmyaḥ samyagjñānenduhṛtprabhaḥ ।। 

māyājālamahodyogaḥ sarvatantrādhipaḥ paraḥ ।
aśeṣavajraparyaṅko niḥśeṣajñānakāyadhṛk ।। 

samantabhadraḥ sumatiḥ kṣitigarbho jagaddhṛtiḥ ।
sarvabuddhamahāgarbho viśvanirmāṇacakradṛk ।। 

sarvabhāvasvabhāvāgyraḥ sarvabhāvasvabhāvadhṛk ।
anutpādadharmā viśvārthaḥ sarvadharmasvabhāvadhṛk ।। 

ekakṣaṇamahāprājñaḥ sarvadharmāvabodhadhṛk ।
sarvadharmābhisamayo bhūtāntamuniragradhīḥ ।। 

stimitaḥ suprasannātmā samyaksaṃbuddhabodhidhṛk ।
pratyakṣaḥ sarvabuddhānāṃ jñānārciḥ suprabhāsvaraḥ ।। 

iti pratyavekṣaṇajñānagāthāḥ dvācatvāriṃśat ।

iṣṭārthasādhakaḥ paraḥ sarvāpāyaviśodhakaḥ ।
sarvasattvottamo nāthaḥ sarvasattvapramocakaḥ ।। 

kleśasaṃgrāmaśūraikaḥ ajñānaripudarpahā ।
dhīśṛṅgāradharaḥ śrīmān vīrabībhatsarupadhṛk ।। 

bāhudaṇḍaśatākṣepapadanikṣepanarttanaḥ ।
śrīmacchatabhujābhogagaganābhoganarttanaḥ ।। 

ekapādatalākrāntamahīmaṇḍatale sthitaḥ ।
brahmāṇḍaśikharākrāntapādāṅguṣṭhanakhe sthitaḥ ।। 

ekārtho advayadharmārthaḥ paramārtho avinaśvaraḥ ।
nānāvijñaptirupārthaścittavijñānasaṃtatiḥ ।। 

aśeṣabhāvārtharatiḥ śūnyatāratiragradhīḥ ।
bhavarāgādyatītaśca bhavatrayamahāratiḥ ।। 

śuddhaḥ śubhrābhradhavalaḥ śaraccandrāṃśusuprabhaḥ ।
bālārkamaṇḍalacchāyo mahārāganakhaprabhaḥ ।। 

indranīlāgrasaccīro mahānīlakacāgradhṛk ।
mahāmaṇimayūkhaśrīrbuddhanirvāṇabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। 

lokadhātuśatākampī ṛddhipādamahākramaḥ ।
mahāsmṛtidharastattvaścatuḥsmṛtisamādhirāṭ ।। 

bodhyaṅgakusumāmodastathāgataguṇodadhiḥ ।
aṣṭāṅgamārganayavit samyaksaṃbuddhamārgavit ।। 

sarvasattvamahāsaṅgo niḥsaṅgo gaganopamaḥ ।
sarvasattvamanojātaḥ sarvasattvamanojavaḥ ।। 

sarvasattvetdriyārthajñaḥ sarvasattvamanoharaḥ ।
pañcaskandhārthatattvajñaḥ pañcaskandhaviśuddhadhṛk ।। 

sarvaniryāṇakoṭisthaḥ sarvaniryāṇakovidaḥ ।
sarvaniryāṇamārgasthaḥ sarvaniryāṇadeśakaḥ ।। 

dvādaśāṅgabhavotkhāto dvādaśākāraśuddhadhṛk ।
catuḥsatyanayākāro aṣṭajñānāvabodhadhṛk ।। 

dvādaśākārasatyārthaḥ ṣoḍaśākāratattvavit ।
viṃśatyākārasaṃbodhirvibuddhaḥ sarvavitparaḥ ।। 

ameyabuddhanirmāṇakāyakoṭivibhāvakaḥ ।
sarvakṣaṇābhisamayaḥ sarvacittakṣaṇārthavit ।। 

nānāyānanayopāyajagadarthavibhāvakaḥ ।
yānatritayaniryāta ekayānaphale sthita ।। 

kleśadhātuviśuddhātmā karmadhātukṣayaṅkaraḥ ।
oghodadhisamuttīrṇo yogakāntāranisṛtaḥ ।। 

kleśopakleśasaṃkleśasuprahīṇasavāsanaḥ ।
prajñopāyamahākaruṇā amoghajagadarthakṛt ।। 

sarvasaṃjñāprahoṇārtho vijñānārtho nirodhakṛt ।
sarvasattvamanoviṣayaḥ sarvasattvamanogatiḥ ।। 

sarvasattvamano antasthastaccittasamatāṅgataḥ ।
sarvasattvamanohlādī sarvasattvamanoratiḥ ।। 

siddhānto vibhramāpetaḥ sarvabhrāntivivarjitaḥ ।
niḥsaṃdigdhamatistryarthaḥ sarvārthastriguṇātmakaḥ ।। 

pañcaskandhārthastrikālaḥ sarvakṣaṇavibhāvakaḥ ।
ekakṣaṇābhisaṃbuddhaḥ sarvabuddhasvabhāvadhṛk ।। 

anaṅgakāyaḥ kāyāgyraḥ kāyakoṭivibhāvakaḥ ।
aśeṣarupasandarśī ratnaketurmahāmaṇiḥ ।। 

iti samatājñānagāthāścaturviśatiḥ ।

sarvasaṃbuddhaboddhavyo buddhabodhiranuttaraḥ ।
anakṣaro mantrayonirmahāmantra kulatrayaḥ ।। 

sarvamantrārthajanako mahābinduranakṣaraḥ ।
pañcākṣaro mahāśūnyo binduśūnyaḥ ṣaḍakṣaraḥ ।। 

sarvākāro nirākāraḥ ṣoḍaśārdhārdhabindudhṛk ।
akalaḥ kalanātīścaturthadhyānakoṭidhṛk ।। 

sarvadhyānakalābhijñaḥ samādhikulagotravit ।
samādhikāyaḥ kāyāgyraḥ sarvasaṃbhogakāyarāṭ ।। 

nirmāṇakāyaḥ kāyāgyro buddhanirmāṇavaṃśadhṛk ।
daśadigviśvanirmāṇo yathāvajjagadarthakṛt ।। 

devātidevo devendraḥ surendro dānavādhipaḥ ।
amarendraḥ suraguruḥ pramathaḥ pramatheśvaraḥ ।। 

uttīrṇabhavakāntāra ekaḥ śāstā jagadguruḥ ।
prakhyātadaśadigloko dharmadānapatirmahān ।। 

maitrīsannāhasannaddhaḥ karuṇāvarmavarmitaḥ ।
prajñākhaḍgo dhanurbāṇaḥ kleśājñānaraṇañjahaḥ ।। 

mārārirmārajidvīraścaturmārabhayāntakṛt ।
sarvamāracamūjetā sambaddho lokanāyakaḥ ।। 

vandyaḥ pūjyo abhivādyaśca mānanīyaśca nityaśaḥ ।
arcanīyatamo mānyo namasyaḥ paramo guruḥ ।। 

trailokyaikakramagatirvyomaparyyantavikramaḥ ।
traividyaḥ śrotriyaḥ pūtaḥ ṣaḍabhijñaḥ ṣaḍanusmṛtiḥ ।। 

bodhisattvo mahāsattvo lokātīto maharddhikaḥ ।
prajñāpāramitāniṣṭhaḥ prajñātattvatvamāgataḥ ।। 

ātmavitparavitsarvaḥ sarvīyo hyagrapudgalaḥ ।
sarvopamāmatikrānto jñeyo jñānādhipaḥ paraḥ ।। 

dharmadānapatiḥ śreṣṭhaścaturmudrārthadeśakaḥ ।
paryupāsyatamo jagatāṃ niryāṇatrayayāyinām ।। 

paramārthaviśuddhaśrīstrailokyasubhago mahān ।
sarvasampatkaraḥ śrīmān mañjuśrīḥ śrīmatāṃvaraḥ ।। 

iti kṛtyānuṣṭhānajñānagāthāḥ pañcadaśa ।

namaste varadavajrāgyra bhūtakoṭe namo astu te ।
namaste śūnyatāgarbha buddhabodhe namostu te ।। 

buddharāga namaste astu buddhakāma namo namaḥ ।
buddhaprīte namastubhyaṃ buddhamoda namo namaḥ ।। 

buddhasmita namastubhyaṃ buddhahāsa namo namaḥ ।
buddhavāca namastubhyaṃ buddhabhāva namo namaḥ ।। 

abhavodbhava namastubhyaṃ namaste buddhasaṃbhava ।
gaganodbhava namastubhyaṃ namaste jñānasaṃbhava ।। 

māyājāla namastubhyaṃ namaste buddhanāṭaka ।
namaste sarvasarvebhyo jñānakāya namo astu te ।।
